Commentary

How to Maintain the Students' Patriotic Movement

Since the beginning of the student patriotic movement, this newspaper has repeatedly discussed it. Recently, the incident of Nankai students going to Beijing to petition was first seen in the northern schools and local authorities, which were bitterly resisted. Later, representatives from the central government rushed to persuade them to return to Tianjin. Following this, Zhejiang University students in Hangzhou were arrested for planning to gather in Beijing, and the president resigned. In Shanghai, Fudan students went to the capital to petition, but were blocked by the authorities at the North Railway Station. The two sides have been deadlocked for a full day and night, and the issue has not yet been resolved. Observing the current situation and worrying about the future, the reporter believes that the most important thing for the central and local authorities in the development of this situation is how to consistently fulfill their responsibility to protect the students. After all, the students are young and full of emotion. They have long been indignant at foreign insults and have been depressed for a long time. Once they vent their anger, it will be difficult to control. Those who bear the responsibility of guidance should completely eliminate their emotions, carefully consider the psychology of young people, and continue to protect them with good intentions, so that no problems will arise and students will be able to accept persuasion.

At this juncture, Jiang, the head of the Executive Yuan, ordered the Ministry of Education to convene principals of colleges and universities above the junior college level and student representatives from provinces and cities with convenient transportation to gather in Beijing to openly declare the government's policies and exchange views on safeguarding the country. If this matter can be realized on schedule, the government will have the opportunity to clarify how to maintain territorial integrity and how to prevent traitors from succeeding, and students will have the opportunity to understand and appreciate this. On the other hand, the students' desire to petition and their ideas for saving the country will also be contributed to the authorities. The reporter recalls the past, that student movements must seek actual results for their petitions to be satisfied. It is difficult to satisfy them with mere words. The reason why the students are bound to go to Beijing to petition is precisely because of this. The Ministry of Education's convening of student representatives to gather in Beijing so that young students and practical politicians can meet together is also a practical result. The central government's intention to maintain the students' patriotic movement in this way should be understood by local authorities.

This determines that the students' patriotic movement is purely out of patriotic enthusiasm and is not mixed with other factors. This can be known from their declarations and slogans, and can be seen from their actions. Therefore, since its launch, the public opinion has responded and people from all walks of life have sympathized with it, which is rare in the past. Even the political authorities are mostly able to understand their intentions and do not obstruct them. As for why it has reached the current situation, it is because the country has reached a point where it is shocking to see and unbearable to endure. Purely rational persuasion has lost its effectiveness. Now, to seek a good result, it depends on the results of the meeting convened by the Ministry of Education. Before the meeting, the local authorities' well-intentioned maintenance of the student movement is essential.

Mutual Assistance of Naval Forces in the Mediterranean: Countries Willing to Support Britain, Turkey, Greece, and Yugoslavia Answer Without Reservations, Spain Hesitates

London: The British government posed questions to the countries along the Mediterranean coast (namely Yugoslavia, Greece, Turkey, Romania, and Spain) earlier this month, stating that if the British Navy is attacked in the Mediterranean, are these countries prepared to provide assistance? It is now known that Greece, Turkey, and Yugoslavia have all replied to Britain, prepared to provide assistance without reservations. Romania said that if Britain requests assistance, it will certainly repay the favor. As for the implementation of naval mutual assistance, British military attaches stationed in these countries will conduct talks with experts from these countries. In addition, Spain's attitude is still hesitant. However, the British government did not directly make a request to it, but the new Foreign Secretary Eden discussed it with the Spanish representative to the League of Nations, Madariaga. As for the mutual assistance arrangements recently discussed by the British and French general staffs, the results are said to be very satisfactory. (Havas dispatch on the 23rd)

Madrid: It is rumored that the British government has posed questions to the Spanish government, stating that if the country's navy is attacked by Italy in the Mediterranean, is Spain prepared to provide assistance? Prime Minister Valladares declared to the press after the cabinet meeting that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs had not received a formal note regarding this matter, and that the cabinet meeting today did not discuss it. (Havas dispatch on the 23rd)

London: Today, it was learned that the British and French naval staffs recently contacted each other on the matter of mutual assistance in the event of an Italian attack on the British fleet. Some members of the British naval staff discussed this matter in Paris a few days ago. According to London sources, the talks were very satisfactory. (Reuters dispatch on the 23rd)

Straits of Tartary: Issue of Fortification, Turkey Asks Britain and France to Lift Treaty Restrictions

Ankara: It is heard that the British and Turkish governments have exchanged official documents to discuss the conditions under which Turkey can cooperate with Britain in the event of war in the Mediterranean. Turkish officials are currently maintaining absolute silence on this matter. However, according to semi-official sources, Turkey has given a satisfactory reply to Britain's inquiry. Other Balkan countries have also given similar replies. It is widely believed that Turkey will take this opportunity to raise again the issue of building fortresses in the Straits of Tartary. (Reuters dispatch on the 24th)

Paris: Madame Taboui, a famous journalist, recently published an article in the Shih-yeh Pao, describing the visit of Turkish Foreign Minister Rustu to Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval yesterday. She said that the purpose, in addition to discussing the issue of the Mediterranean security organization, also involved the issue of the country's fortification of the Straits of Tartary. Because the Turkish government intends to request the British government to abolish the provisions of the 1923 Treaty of Lausanne that forbid the fortification of the Straits of Tartary. When Rustu met with Laval yesterday, he must have requested France to support this request. According to Madame Taboui, "Turkey has been preoccupied with this matter for a long time. As far as we know, the country has long been looking forward to the British government's understanding. Now that Britain has raised the issue of collective security in the Mediterranean, Turkey will naturally consider this opportunity to be one in a thousand, and will take the opportunity to raise the issue of fortification of the Straits of Tartary. We firmly believe that the British government will provide a satisfactory response. As for the French government, it will probably answer that if Britain accepts Turkey's request, then France will not raise any objections. Regarding the French aid to the British Navy in the Mediterranean, Madame Taboui believes that the French government is prepared to make some arrangements, but no decision has been made at this time. As for the oil embargo, once Britain decides to implement it, what attitude France will take is also undecided at this time. (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

Attitude Towards the Baltic Sea: Britain Gives No Clear Reply, Soviet Union and Other Countries Dissatisfied

London: It is heard that Soviet Russia and the countries along the Baltic Sea will pose questions to the British government, asking what attitude Britain intends to take in response if Germany dominates the Baltic Sea? Although it is not possible to know exactly how the British government's reply is worded, it is known from this newspaper's visit to Chang that the British reply has not been considered satisfactory by the countries concerned, including Soviet Russia. Britain has used the pretext that the above questions are purely hypothetical and future situations, and therefore refuses to give a clear reply. (Note: Britain recently posed questions to the countries along the Mediterranean coast, stating that if the British Navy is attacked in the Mediterranean, are these countries prepared to provide assistance?) (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

Eden Takes Over as Foreign Secretary, First Measure is to Prevent European War, Hoare Goes to Switzerland for Long-Term Recuperation

London: Eden entered Sandringham Palace this morning to meet with the British Emperor, talked briefly, and then, during the Privy Council meeting, respectfully received the seal of the Foreign Office. He is scheduled to take office as Foreign Secretary tomorrow, and then leave London for a few days of recuperation, but he will still be in contact with the ministry at any time. French Prime Minister Laval sent a telegram of congratulations, which included the line, "I am very happy to work with you to promote the common friendship and peace of our two countries." Former Foreign Secretary Hoare and his wife flew from Croydon Airport to Zurich, Switzerland, today. When asked before leaving whether he would return to the government after a short rest, Hoare replied that he could not talk about his future today. (Reuters dispatch on the 23rd)

London: Today it was learned that Eden's first step after taking office as the new Foreign Secretary will be to find ways to reduce the danger of an Anglo-Italian war. Now that Britain has obtained guarantees from Mediterranean countries to back Britain in the event of an Italian attack, the British fleet in the Mediterranean will probably withdraw some units soon. Today, the British Emperor summoned Eden to Sandringham Palace and personally bestowed the seal of the Foreign Office. It is understood that Eden has at least temporarily shelved the oil embargo and its severe economic sanctions measures, because this can both satisfy the British people's demands for severely punishing Italy and also take into account the domestic calls for avoiding war. Now the government has regained the guarantees of cooperation with Britain from Turkey, Greece, Yugoslavia, Romania, Spain, and Egypt, in addition to France. (National dispatch on the 23rd)

London: Political figures believe that after the new Foreign Secretary Eden takes office, he may not intensify the sanctions policy against Italy. Even if he does intensify it, it must wait until mid-January next year. In general, people believe that Eden will not take drastic action against Italy. Britain's attitude will depend on the development of the war in Africa. A message was received here from Rome that Italy has failed halfway in the war in East Africa. The general staff of the expeditionary force has decided to change its tactics, and will advance in a guerrilla manner thereafter, and suspend the activities of the mechanized units. (Havas dispatch on the 23rd) Zurich, Switzerland: Former British Foreign Secretary Sir Samuel Hoare and his wife recently flew to this place from London, where the doctor advised him to rest for a long time. (Havas dispatch on the 23rd)

London: Prime Minister Baldwin has left London today for Chequers, West Wycombe, to spend the Christmas and New Year holidays. (Reuters dispatch on the 23rd)

Rome Decides Not to Reply to British and French Peace Proposals, French Ambassador Visits Italian Foreign Ministry

Italian Newspapers Criticize British Policy, Saying It Could Endanger European Peace

Rome. A semi-official Italian newspaper published an article proving that the policies adopted by Britain are sufficient to endanger peace. In brief, the British government is deliberately adopting a policy hostile to Italy and is not seeking a solution to the dispute. Its purpose is nothing more than to automatically create a threat of war in order to use it as an excuse to attack Italy. From this point of view, it is clear that the point of conflict is between Britain and Italy, and not between Italy and the League of Nations. The newspaper also said that the development of the situation shows that countries will repeat the same mistakes by cooperating with the League of Nations. "We have seen various international elements, red, green, black, and grey, all becoming active again, instigating incidents, and hating our country's colonial rights, and dragging all European countries to take crazy actions against Italy. These elements that are disrupting European security are now striding forward, full of hope to achieve their ambitions. It must be known that the Third International knows that the implementation of sanctions against various countries will inevitably cause a major disaster in Europe. It can then take the opportunity to rise up, and its activity will be doubled compared to before. In short, Europe is now in a state of chaos, dark and unseen. All that can be seen is a path leading to destruction. It is difficult to foresee where it will end." (Havas dispatch on the 23rd)

Rome. The Italian People's Newspaper, the official newspaper of the Prime Minister, recently published that "the cruel means of the countries that have implemented sanctions against Italy have brought about the threat of war to Europe. Where should European countries go? It is appropriate to choose for themselves, because people have reached this crossroads and should each shoulder their responsibilities to the brilliant world of history and civilization. Italy has the full right to test whether the peace proposals put forward by former British Foreign Secretary Hoare and French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval are strong and unbreakable. However, before the Fascist Supreme Council decided on its attitude, this proposal suffered a fatal blow. This responsibility should not be borne by Italy." The newspaper then criticized the British government's contact with Mediterranean countries on the 8th of this month to discuss war against Italy (i.e., asking these countries whether they could provide naval assistance when the British navy was threatened by the Italian navy), saying, "Britain proposes peace proposals to Italy on the one hand, and at the same time, or even before, asks Mediterranean countries to form an alliance in preparation for war against Italy. How can these two things be reconciled? Who would believe that Britain is not deceiving Europe? Britain has issued a general naval mobilization order in the Mediterranean, what is its intention? If the League of Nations does not allow it, Britain urgently requires the Mediterranean countries to expand their mobilization scope. If it is not with the permission of the League of Nations, then on what principle is it doing so?" (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

Libyan Border: Italian and Ethiopian Soldiers Clash; Egyptian Authorities Deny It, But the Situation Remains Tense

Cairo. Rumors that Italian and Ethiopian soldiers clashed on the Libyan border have been denied by the Egyptian Ministry of Military Affairs today. However, the rumors have been circulating for a long time, and the denial has only been made now, leading observers to believe that the clash may not be completely fabricated. After the news of the clash spread, there was great unease here, especially among the public. The government's order to extend the service period of 1,200 reservists has further increased the tension. (National Telegram on the 23rd)

Abyssinian Army's Clever Strategy Defeats the Enemy: Using Scarecrows to Lure the Enemy Deep, Italian Soldiers Fall into an Ambush and Are Slaughtered

Abyssinian Capital. The Abyssinian army in the north recently won a great victory over the Italian army in the Danbian area, near Adia Bi, using a clever strategy and capturing tanks. The tactic used was to place a large number of scarecrows in white clothes in the positions, which looked like soldiers from a distance. When Italian aircraft scouted the area, they immediately dropped bombs and destroyed them. The tanks and infantry in the rear, believing that the remaining enemies here had been wiped out, also advanced, unaware that the Abyssinian troops were all wearing their native brown uniforms and hiding on nearby hills. When the Italian army went deep, they were suddenly surrounded and slaughtered, and ten tanks were captured. (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

Fierce Battle in the Danbian Area: Intense Artillery Fire Followed by Hand-to-Hand Combat; Abyssinian Army Resists Forcefully but is Eventually Defeated

Rome. According to a communiqué, an Italian and Eritrean mixed brigade fought a major battle with 5,000 Abyssinian soldiers near Adia Bi in the Danbian area and defeated them. The intensity of the Italian artillery bombardment was the first decisive battle on the northern front since the start of the war on October 3. The Abyssinian army attempted to flank the left wing of the Italian army. The Italian army counterattacked, followed by fierce hand-to-hand combat with bayonets and Abyssinian knives and gun stocks. The Italian army had mountain artillery, aircraft, and machine guns to help. As a result, the Abyssinian army retreated to the Tongzhua Valley and eventually fled. The Italian and Eritrean soldiers pursued them. The terrain advanced by the Italian army was rugged and sometimes impassable. The Italian artillery was ambushed behind the hills and was still able to bombard the Abyssinian positions with artillery shells. This battle drove the Abyssinian army out of a forty-square-mile fertile land that produced grain. This is one of the main sources of food supply in the Danbian area, so the Abyssinian army may feel the difficulty of military food from now on. According to official announcements, 600 Abyssinian soldiers were killed and 1,000 were wounded. Two Italian white officers and three Eritrean officers were killed, and 100 Eritrean soldiers were wounded. Italian aircraft inflicted heavy damage on the enemy. (Reuters dispatch on the 23rd)

Italy Protests to the League of Nations for the Second Time, Accusing the Abyssinian Army of Using Dumdum Bullets

London. Italian Foreign Minister Suweichu yesterday submitted a second protest to League of Nations Secretary-General 爱文诺 regarding the use of dumdum bullets by the Abyssinian army, and said that these dumdum bullets were produced by the Erin factory in England. Officials here have formally denied this statement, saying that British manufacturers have never sold these bullets to Abyssinia. The Italian protest has not yet been sent to the British government. (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

Italians Eagerly Donate Gold to the Country; More Than 600 Kilograms Have Been Collected

Naples. Crown Prince Bimon donated all of his "Annunziata" class gold necklaces to the country, which have now been melted into pure gold. In addition, the Prince also donated three gold bars, with different colors, one white and one red, weighing a total of four and a half kilograms. Since the start of the fundraising campaign, the Naples Provincial Fascist Party Headquarters has raised 621 kilograms of gold and 150,000 gold wedding rings. (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

Austrian Prime Minister's Broadcast Speech: Striving to Maintain Peace; Christmas Amnesty for Political Prisoners

Vienna. State Prime Minister Xiushuni delivered a Christmas speech on radio last night, announcing to the people of the whole country, stating that the new Austria's aspiration lies in maintaining peace, and in terms of the current national strength, it is sufficient to work hard for peace in all aspects. As for the amnesty order issued by the government on Christmas, the number of political prisoners pardoned is as follows: Regarding the Social Democratic Party members who were arrested for participating in the February 1934 riots, the total number is 170. It is decided to release 154 of them. The other 16 are not included in the amnesty because they committed murder. The prosecution of 19 cadres of the party, who were originally intended to be prosecuted by the court, will also be stopped due to the amnesty. Regarding the members of the National Socialist Party who were implicated in the assassination of the late Prime Minister Dollfuss in July last year, 16 of them with lighter circumstances will also be released. There are also 955 people who were sentenced by the court for administrative errors, and they will also be granted probation. In addition, there are 170 prisoners in detention camps in various places, and 125 prisoners who participated in the assassination of the late Prime Minister Dollfuss, who are not included in the amnesty because of their serious crimes. (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

Germany's Newly Built Escort Ships; Six Join the Naval Service

Kiel, Germany. Six newly built naval escort ships have started service today. Each warship has a displacement of 600 tons and is equipped with four 105mm caliber cannons, four 37mm caliber anti-aircraft guns, and two anti-aircraft machine guns. Another four similar escort ships will be built in the Hamburg port shipyard. (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

Famous American Aviator Lindbergh Flees to England; Secretly Leaves the Country Temporarily After Repeatedly Receiving Threatening Letters; One Theory is to Discuss Atlantic Aviation Matters

New York. The news of the Lindberghs' trip to England with their children surprised the whole country. Readers initially suspected that the statement was inaccurate. Later, they learned that the Lindberghs and their three children had indeed departed on a ship that was scheduled to arrive in Liverpool on December 30. Lindbergh's departure was extremely secretive. Even his mother, who currently lives in Troy, did not know about it. Lindbergh often received threatening letters about kidnapping and killing his young son, so he made a plan to move to a better place. According to a friend closely related to the Lindbergh family in Eagle, New Jersey, Lindbergh does not want to live in England forever. However, according to reliable sources, Lindbergh does not want to return to the country until the Hauptmann case has been forgotten. A few hours after the news of Lindbergh's trip to England spread, Hauptmann immediately submitted a petition for pardon to the New Jersey pardon office. Its contents have not yet been revealed. According to the plan, Hauptmann's death sentence will be carried out within one week starting on January 13, 1936. (Reuters dispatch on the 23rd)

New York. The famous aviator Colonel Lindbergh recently set off for England with his wife and three-year-old child. Although his whereabouts were extremely secretive, they were still known to the newspapers. Speculation about Lindbergh's motives for this action is nothing more than the following: Lindbergh recently received many threatening letters, all threatening to kill his young son. He has been like a frightened bird since the kidnapping of his beloved son three years ago, so he moved overseas to avoid it. The kidnapper Hauptmann is scheduled to be executed on January 13, so he went abroad before the execution and will return to the country afterward. The Governor of New Jersey decided to request a retrial of the Hauptmann case. Lindbergh believed that the case had been infiltrated by political issues and could not be brought out again, so he decided to go abroad. In addition, there is another theory that Lindbergh's trip is to England to discuss the establishment of regular Atlantic aviation services. Pan American Airways confirmed that Lindbergh had indeed gone to Europe and will continue to serve as a technical consultant for the company. The State Department declined to comment on Lindbergh's trip. (Havas dispatch on the 23rd)

London. The famous American aviator Colonel Lindbergh set off from New York yesterday with his wife and three-year-old child to come to England. It is said that he will live in South Wales. The members of the local society have attracted great attention when they heard the news. (Havas dispatch on the 24th)

En Route to Honolulu, the China Clipper Battles a Storm; Forced to Turn Back to Alameda

Alameda. The newly established trans-Pacific airmail service has now encountered its first setback. The China Clipper flew from here to Honolulu yesterday. At 5:18 this morning, it flew back here, battling storms in the sky for fourteen hours. However, because the weather showed no signs of improving, it was decided to fly back to wait. (Reuters dispatch on the 23rd)

America's Alarming Debt; Reaching One-Fifth of the Nation's Wealth

New York. The board of directors of the National Industrial Conference Board stated today that the public debt of the United States Federal Government and state governments has reached 500 billion US dollars. In 1932, it was only 390 billion US dollars. The total public debt has reached one-fifth of the nation's wealth. Interest payments account for as much as 20% of all government revenue. The department said that the trend of increasing public debt is a serious problem for the country. In addition, five-sixths of the new debts issued by the Federal Government are absorbed by national banks. In fact, this situation is expansion. (National Telegram on the 23rd)

Incident of Japanese and Puppet Troops Committing Atrocities Across the Border; Outer Mongolian Authorities File a Protest; Demanding Punishment of the Culprits, Compensation, and an Apology

Moscow. Moscow newspapers published a report from Kulun that the Acting Prime Minister of the Mongolian Republic, 丙阁, and Acting Foreign Minister Zhuobusan telegraphed a protest to the Foreign Minister of "Manchukuo" regarding the armed looting of the Mongolian border by Japanese and "Manchu" troops on December 19. They said that the Japanese and "Manchu" troops killed and captured 16 Hao Gu border guards. They continued to say that the government of the Mongolian Republic protested most resolutely against the actions of the Japanese and "Manchu" troops, that is, the illegal invasion of the Mongolian border by the Japanese and "Manchu" troops, and the killing of Hao Gu border guards, and the destruction of the property of the Mongolian state. At the same time, they also demanded that the "Manchu government" immediately return the captured soldiers, investigate this incident, severely punish the personnel responsible for directing this attack, compensate for the destroyed and looted property, and finally, the "Manchu government" should formally apologize for this incident and guarantee that such looting of the Mongolian Republic's border will not happen again in the future. The protest letter recounted that in the Manzhouli Conference, the Mongolian government strongly advocated the establishment of a border mixed committee to resolve and prevent various border disputes, but "Manchu" expressed opposition to this proposal and continued to attack the border policy, attempting to forcibly occupy Mongolian territory. The Mongolian Republic 政府 thought it reasonable to warn the "Manchu government" that if the sudden attack by the Japanese and "Manchu" troops on the Mongolian Republic 引 caused serious results, the "Manchu" and Japanese governments should be fully responsible, because their troops directly and proactively participated in such attacks. (TASS dispatch on the 24th)

Tokyo. Regarding the dispute between the troops of the two countries that occurred west of Lake 波衣尔 in the "Manchu"-Mongolian border on the 19th of this month, the Outer Mongolian Foreign Minister had protested to the "Manchukuo" government on the 22nd regarding this matter, demanding an apology, compensation, and future guarantees. According to the information issued by the local army to the Central Army Department, it is known that this Outer Mongolian government's protest is not true at all. The "Manchukuo" side had, at the Manzhouli Conference, in order to prevent border disputes and to establish friendly relations between the two countries, advocated sincerity. However, the Outer Mongolian side was greatly restrained by the Soviet forces behind it, causing the conference to break down. This was a disaster caused by not seeing each other with sincerity. The "Manchukuo" side, based on the determination expressed at the time of the conference's breakdown, aimed to substantially determine the 界, and is now dispatching a team to investigate, learning that the Outer Mongolian troops who crossed the border and occupied the area illegally overstepped their authority and caused a conflict. The "Manchukuo" government, based on this fact, decided to ignore the Outer Mongolian protest. At the same time, if the Outer Mongolian side still refuses to acknowledge the negotiations to determine the border, it points out that the dispute is likely to occur frequently and urges them to reflect deeply. The Central Army Department attaches great importance to this situation in ensuring the security of the "Manchukuo" border. (United Dispatch on the 24th)

London Silver Group Formed to Assist in Absorbing Futures; Silver Market Expected to Stabilize

London. It was learned today that a silver group has been organized here by a manager of a large bank in New York to assist the silver market in accepting the current forward contracts due in London. This will enable the silver market to properly dispose of the spot goods, and brokers can also breathe a sigh of relief. Because most of the recent futures sales were from banks in the Far East, the contracts could not be cancelled, and brokers were greatly troubled. Now that there is a silver group to absorb them, everyone hopes that the trend can be slightly stabilized. (National Agency dispatch on the 23rd)

American Silver Faction Senators Optimistic About the Trend of the Silver Market

Washington. Senators from the silver faction of Senator Pittman's party stated today that they do not value the declining world silver prices. A spokesman for the faction said that they did hear that domestically mined silver would definitely be sold at a good price, and that world silver prices might return to their original state in the future. The current decline in world silver prices is what he considers one aspect of the optimistic overall situation. (National Telegram on the 23rd)

Washington. Silver faction senators close to the government stated today that the U.S. Treasury Department intends to maintain the silver price of newly mined domestic silver, or even raise the silver price to $1.29 per ounce. Because the general election is approaching, the government will continue to support silver prices. World silver prices will depend on the total silver inventory in the market and the development in various places. In short, the faction is indifferent to the current trend in the world silver market. (National Telegram on the 23rd)

U.S. Recovery Administration; All Offices Closed; Commercial Cooperation and Consumption Departments Merged into the Department of Commerce and Industry

Washington. President Roosevelt today ordered the closure of the Recovery Administration. After the Supreme Court ruled that the Recovery Act was unconstitutional, the bureau only maintained the remaining situation with a skeleton organization. After the closure, only the Commercial Cooperation Department will be merged into the Department of Commerce and continue to work. The activities of the Consumer Department will be transferred to the Department of Labor. (National Telegram on the 23rd)

Two hundred miles of land from Brighton to the south coast is shrouded in fog. Many places are impassable. Trains are delayed and flights are suspended. Many people who travel by car because of the slippery and dangerous roads change to trains. Shipping is also blocked. There were many accidents yesterday, with many deaths and injuries. Three men and a boy drowned while ice skating. (Reuters dispatch on the 24th)

They looted 7,000 yuan in cash, with the total value of stolen goods estimated at 10,000 yuan. No one was injured. On the morning of the 22nd, at Hailufeng, the robbers disembarked onto a sailboat,绑 tying up passenger Li Xinghao of the Lixing Company, Dongjiang, and his son, Fuqiang, and taking them away. Investigating the Truth of the Anxi Iron Mine

Xiamen. After arriving in Xiamen, Zhao Xiujin, the director of the Anxi Iron Mine Exploration Project Office, issued a written statement. The Anxi iron ore deposits are rich, and the quality of Panshan ore is good. However, Panshan is located in high mountains, making transportation difficult. Exploration will first determine the ore reserves and assess whether they are worth mining. At the same time, transportation routes will be studied. Mineral exploration will take ten months, and railway and harbor surveys will take two to three months. If mining is deemed worthwhile, all further actions will be decided by the central government. The exploration will receive full technical assistance. Whether we will undertake the mining in the future and how to raise capital will not be discussed until the amount of ore and transportation issues are clarified. As for renting machinery and hiring Japanese technicians, previous requests were submitted to Jiang Zai and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for approval. Chen Hongsheng, the Foreign Affairs Section Chief of the Provincial Government, also came along and spoke, dispelling external doubts. At the same time, the Construction Department issued an explanation in the province with the same intention. Zhao stated that diamond drilling machines for mineral exploration are very expensive and are also being rented from Japan. The technicians have already arrived. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Discussions on Economic Affairs

— Edited by Tang Qingzeng

Chinese Silk

— Qian Tianda

Sericulture in our country has a history of thousands of years. The area for raising silkworms and producing silk is almost the same size as our country's territory. It is indeed one of the most common and important side occupations in rural areas, and it occupies an important position in foreign trade. Since the failure of the silk industry, the rural economy has collapsed, the urban economy has declined, and the entire national economy has been affected, facing the danger of total collapse. However, due to the unstable domestic political situation and the withering of various industries, this serious problem has not been noticed by the people of the country. Although improvement associations and other organizations have been established, they are limited by power and financial resources, and cannot achieve the ideal effect of control. Now, a brief description of the failure of the silk industry in our country and its importance is made to attract the attention of the people of the country and provide reference for those who are concerned about the silk industry and the national economy.

It is said that the earliest exports of silk from our country were finished products, such as silk paintings. As the textile industry developed in foreign countries, the export of silk raw materials exceeded the trend of silk goods. However, at this time, both silk raw materials and silk goods were handicrafts. It was not until 1867 that Chen Qiyuan of Guangdong Province created a new silk factory, changing the old handicrafts into mechanical industries. At this point, China's silk industry began to show signs of improvement. (In Shanghai, Huang Zuoqing established a factory on the bank of the North Suzhou River in 1881 (the seventh year of the Guangxu era), named Gonghe Yong. Later, Wuxi Yuchang Silk Factory and others were established one after another.) However, since the beginning of the 20th century, Japan suddenly rose to compete, refining with scientific methods and operating with new machinery. The output was large and the silk quality was good. European and American countries competed to purchase it. During this period, the silk industry in our country not only did not have an active and enterprising spirit, but also adhered to old methods and stood still. At that time, the government did not have a strict commodity inspection system, and delayed and erred, which led to the overseas market being given away with both hands and being unable to be saved, which is a pity.

Table of the Decreasing Trend of Raw Silk Exports in the Last Ten Years

After 1929, the world economic panic broke out, and the purchasing power of various countries decreased. The sales of Chinese silk were further reduced. Although the price of silver fell during this period, it still did not help exports. After Japan re-embargoed gold in 1931, it relied on the fall in currency prices and its government's strong subsidies. Therefore, although Japanese silk exports were in this deep abyss of panic, they were still able to barely support it. However, Chinese silk was even more left behind at this point. In the 19th year of the Republic of China, the highest price of silk from the Shanghai B-character factory was 1,150 taels per load, and the lowest price was 880 taels. It can be seen that since the 19th year, the price of silk has begun to decline. Therefore, there was a request to the government to issue public bonds to save the critical situation. After repeated petitions from silk merchants, the government approved the exemption of export taxes and the issuance of 8 million yuan in public bonds to provide relief, with one-quarter for improving sericulture, one-quarter for improving silk factory equipment, and two-quarters for Jiangzhe silk factories to implement relief. After the January 28th Incident in the 21st year, the market was sluggish, and the domestic silk industry felt that it could not be maintained. The price of silk even fell to 540 taels, sales were stagnant, and inventory increased. Silk merchants felt even more unable to turn around, so there was a second issuance of public bonds to register old silk and old cocoons, and to reward the export of raw silk by 100 yuan per load, and to exempt minor customs duties. This measure was completed in the spring of the 32nd year, but this method was only a temporary expedient, and it was also a drop in the bucket, which did not help the progress of the entire silk industry. In March and April of the 23rd year (1934), the sales of Chinese silk showed a slight boom due to the increase in prices in the United States, and the price also increased accordingly. People were praying that it would rise like Qingyun. Unexpectedly, after autumn, it fell again and could not recover. The selling price was low and sales were even more stagnant. Manufacturers suffered heavily. This spring (24th year), the United States implemented a silver purchasing policy, and the price of silver increased rapidly, from about 30 cents per ounce to more than 70 cents. The export of Chinese silk was further hindered, and the market price fell to 400 yuan. The silk industry was almost in a state of no return. After the spring cocoons came on the market, the silk market gradually progressed, and it has risen about twice as much from the lowest price. The implementation of the new currency policy has made the domestic silk price rise even more due to the sharp contraction of foreign exchange. The number of exports has also greatly increased. From June to October this year, 20,000 bales have been exported. Looking at the increasing consumption of raw silk in the United States recently, the future of Chinese silk is indeed promising. Not only can international trade reverse the decline, but the rural economy is also like a life-saving elixir. The rural economy of our country has always relied on side occupations other than crop harvests for adjustment. In the rural areas of the provinces in the Yellow River Basin, the side occupations of farmers are not very developed, so they are not as prosperous as those in the rural areas of Jiangzhe. Among the rural side occupations, sericulture is the most profitable. Outside of Jiangzhe, such as Sichuan, Guangdong, and Shandong, there are also many farming families who rely on the harvest of spring orchids to make ends meet, and even their clothing, food, and housing are mostly dependent on this. It is only because there is a lack of accurate statistical materials to prove it, so it has not been noticed by the general public. As for the importance of the position of our country's silk industry in foreign trade, there is no need to elaborate. By reading the following two concise tables, it can be understood;

Comparative Table of Important Export Goods (Unit: Million Customs Taels)

From the above two tables, it can be seen that the importance of raw silk in foreign trade is that it can increase national wealth in a positive aspect, and can also offset some debts and balance international expenditures in a passive aspect. Since the failure of Chinese tea, foreign trade has almost entirely relied on raw silk for replenishment. Therefore, the position of raw silk is even more important. The implementation of the new currency policy and exchange rate management are the prelude to controlling international trade. We deeply hope that foreign trade can gradually develop under the stable policy of the new exchange rate, and we also hope that the international balance of payments will tend to be balanced under the conditions of reduced imports and increased exports.

Wuhan Students' Parade Comes to an End; Wuchang Students Cross the River in Two Days; On the Way Home, They Go to the Construction Department and Destroy Items

A dispatch from Hankou states that all students from secondary and higher schools in Wuhan have held large-scale demonstrations and parades for several days. Due to the Construction Department's suspension of ferry services, they camped out on the riverbank, enduring hunger and cold. Their intense patriotic sentiments have greatly excited the people of Wuhan. Pacification Commissioner He Chengjun, Acting Provincial Chairman Lu Zhu, Education Director Cheng Qibao, Mayor Wu Zhen, Garrison Commander Chen Jicheng, and others believed that the students' actions were driven purely by patriotic fervor and that it would be difficult to stop them as long as they strictly observed discipline. Therefore, they agreed to allow Wuchang students to cross the river in batches on the 22nd and 23rd to parade. The students' goal was thus completely achieved. At 9:00 AM on the 22nd, it was stipulated that the first batch of students from schools crossing the river should gather at the Hanyangmen. This included Wuhan University, Huazhong University, Art College, Sanchu Middle School, Experimental School, Anhui Middle School, Dajiang Middle School, Shandao Girls' Middle School, Chengda Girls' Middle School, Provincial No. 1 Girls' Middle School, Wuchang Women's Vocational School, Wuchang Normal School, Linghu Middle School, Jingnan Middle School, Provincial Senior Business School, Wuchang Junior High School, Wenhua Library School, Bowen Middle School, Zhangchu Middle School, and 19 other schools, totaling more than 2,000 people. They took the Pu'an, Jianhan, and Canghan ferries from the Hanyangmen wharf and landed at the Wangjiagang wharf in Hankou. Students from Hankou Yixun Girls' Middle School, St. Cana's Girls' Middle School, and other schools warmly welcomed them on the riverbank. They then joined the parade, electing a representative from Wuhan University as the general commander and a representative from Huazhong University as the deputy commander. They started from Wangjiagang, passed through Minquan Road, Sanmin Road, the Municipal Government, Jisheng Fourth Road, Sanma Road, Liudu Bridge, Minsheng Road, and reached the Jianghan Customs. They shouted slogans along the way, which were both tragic and passionate. The onlookers on both sides were like walls, all clapping to show their sympathy. The traffic was temporarily cut off wherever they passed, and the police reinforced their posts to maintain order. In addition to distributing leaflets along the way, the propaganda team also gave simple speeches. Many citizens were moved to tears. At 1:30 PM, the entire group arrived at the Jianghan Customs, where the audience was even more crowded. The students' slogans to save the country shook the mountains and made them feel even more excited. After the parade, they took the Jianhan and other ferries back to Wuchang from Wharf 1. Elementary school students also organized a慰劳 team to welcome them at Hanyangmen and distributed food. Around 3:00 PM, they dispersed and returned to their respective schools. The second batch of students was scheduled to cross the river on the 23rd. Cheng Qibao, the Director of Education, made a speech on this student movement, saying, "Since this patriotic movement of students was launched in Beiping, Tianjin, Nanjing, Shanghai, Wuhan, and Changsha, this is also a manifestation of the patriotic sentiments of young students based on their conscience. The education authorities have nothing to criticize. However, young people are full of vigor and must suppress their temporary emotions and use reason to engage in this kind of movement. Every move should be in line with the norm. Today's difficult national situation does not allow otherwise. Moreover, the work of saving the country cannot be accomplished in a day or two. If valuable time is wasted for a long time, it will not only not help the country, but also damage personal studies, which is also a loss to the country. Therefore, Minister Wang of the Ministry of Education urged 'saving the country through reading' in his telegram to the educational circles. This is what I hope from the students in Wuhan. The various actions of the students in Wuhan in the past few days have fully demonstrated their patriotism, and the request of the students in Wuchang to cross the river has also been fulfilled. Each school should resume classes as usual from today."

A continuing dispatch states that the second batch of students from Zhonghua University, Education College, Wenhua Middle School, Wenhua Second Division, Dagong Middle School, Wuchang Vocational School, Qunhua Middle School, Rural Normal School, Second Girls' Middle School, Enan Middle School, Wuchang Middle School, Lve Enan Hunan Women's Vocational School, Yuije Middle School, Zhangchu Middle School, Chucai Middle School, Provincial High School, Qihuang Middle School, Wenhua Middle School, Higher Agriculture, Wuhan University Agriculture, and 21 other schools, with more than 8,000 students, crossed the river on the 23rd! At nine o'clock, the second batch crossed the Han River on the Baolong, Wu'an, Jianhan, and Canghan ferries. The students from Hankou participating included Xinmian Girls' Middle School, Zizhi Middle School, Boxue Middle School, Guanghua Middle School, Zhongxue Middle School, and five other schools. The students from Hanyang Higher Industry, Xun Girls' Middle School, Hanyang Junior High School, and Xiaozhi Middle School, four schools, lined up around the statue of President Sun Yat-sen on Sanmin Road to wait. When the Wuchang Hankou student contingents passed by, they joined the group, totaling more than 10,000 people. The parade route first followed the regulations of the 22nd, passing through Minquan Road, Sanmin Road, the Municipal Government Road. When reaching Zhongshan Road, the route was temporarily changed and passed through Jiaotong Road and then Hualou, and then returned to Minsheng Road. Later, some students wanted to express opposition to a certain store and requested to exit Hualou, passing through Jianghan Road to Jianghan Customs. Many people tried to dissuade them at the time, but the students were extremely excited and even sat on the ground, intending not to move forward. Therefore, the parade still exited Hualou, passed through Jianghan Road, and reached Wharf 1. During this section, the military police were heavily guarded and the students shouted the most impassioned slogans. Photographers along the way had their cameras taken away by the students. At 1:30 PM, more than 10,000 students arrived in front of Jianghan Customs and shouted slogans together for half an hour. The Wuhan students bid farewell to the Hankou and Hanyang students and returned south by boat. On the way back, they passed the Construction Department. Due to the department's suspension of ferry services, the group went to question the director of the Construction Department, Liu Shoupeng. Liu avoided meeting them, and some items in the department were destroyed, but it did not cause any incidents. The student movement in Wuhan will come to an end here. (23rd)

The Only Sugar Manufacturing Enterprise: Jinan Puyi Sugar Factory; Daily Production Capacity of 120,000 Jin of Sugar; Shortage of Raw Materials Cannot Meet Demand

A dispatch from Jinan states that our country's sugar consumption largely relies on Britain and Japan. Customs statistics show that the value of foreign sugar imported annually is 130 million yuan. Our country has only three sugar beet sugar factories: Jinan Puyi Factory, Sichuan, and Guangdong, etc. Among these three, Puyi is the largest. The factory was originally organized by former Beiping Mayor Yuan Liang and others, with a capital of more than 5 million yuan. The initial equipment cost 3.5 million yuan, with the machinery alone reaching 2 million yuan. It was large in scale and the machinery was new. It was founded in the tenth year of the Republic of China. Unfortunately, the manager was not the right person, and the sales were blocked by the war, which led to its closure. Last year, Yuan Liang again contacted Sun Lianzhong and others to raise capital to revive it. The old shareholders used the machinery as a valuation of 1.2 million yuan, and a certain amount of new shares were added to purchase sugar beet seeds and distribute them to farmers to plant. On the one hand, technicians were hired to sort out the machinery. Now that the sugar beets have been harvested and transported, the factory has started manufacturing. On the 15th of this month, products have been transported to the market for sale, and it has been decided to open up sales in the western region in order to recover a part of the profits. It is a pity that there have been frequent disasters this year, and the sugar beet harvest has been poor, failing to reach the expected number. The harvested sugar beets are only enough for about one month of use. Once the raw materials are used up, they will have to change course and manufacture alcohol (the factory has an alcohol factory). They will wait until next year to promote planting again. Our country's sugar market has been occupied by imported goods for decades. The people of the country are eager to make their own sugar. It is expected that the future development of the factory is unlimited. The current situation of the factory is recorded as follows:

Raw material planting sugar beets are mostly of the radish class. The seeds are purchased in Germany. This summer, the factory distributed them to farmers for planting. The range is in the upper and lower reaches of the Yellow River and on both sides of the Xiaoqing River. Originally, 25,000 mu were planted. Unexpectedly, disasters came frequently, first drought and then floods, leaving only more than 10,000 mu. Each mu produces 3,000 jin to 5,000 jin of sugar beets. Because farmers did not have much faith in the factory before, the factory set the price in advance when planting this year. Each 1,000 jin delivered to the factory is priced at 8 yuan. For those who do not deliver, the freight is deducted according to the distance of the road. Seeds are sold to farming households at 1 yuan and 3 jiao per jin. Those who prepay fertilizer costs 3 jiao per jin, and those who do not prepay fertilizer costs 1 jiao per jin. The price of seeds and fertilizers are deducted from the vegetable price. On average, each farming household can earn a net profit of more than 20 yuan per mu after expenses, which is much more profitable than planting other grains. This year, 10,000 mu of sugar beets were planted throughout the province, totaling a profit of more than 200,000 yuan, which is a small supplement to the poor rural economy. They have now been harvested and are being transported to Jinan one after another. Because most of the planters are by the river, they are mostly transported by boat, and others are transported to the factory by donkeys and carts, shoulder to shoulder, which is like a downtown area.

Sugar making procedure

After the sugar beets arrive at the factory, they are first transported by light vehicles to the weighing place. After weighing, they are transported into a brick-built rectangular pool. Because there is a lot of mud, the factory opened a ditch from the Xiaoqing River behind the factory and diverted water into the yard. The workers use iron shovels to put the sugar beets into the water for rinsing. The water flow is very rapid, and the impact of the water is used to flush the sugar beets into the factory building. Then, a waterwheel is used to rotate the sugar beets into the upper iron trough. After being washed again, it is mechanically transported to the weighing device upstairs. Every 5,000 jin is automatically leaked down. Then, those who accept the leaked down from the weighing device start to build into thin strips, and then transport the thin strips to the upper floor and put them into dozens of round steam pots to dissolve and boil three times, and then turn them into a white thick liquid. The slag is transported to the outside of the factory through iron pipes. The liquid is the raw material for sugar making, and it is put into the sugar boiling pot for decoction. After passing through more than a dozen sugar boiling pots, the heat is gradually increased until the most extreme, and then it becomes an English red thick liquid, shaped like honey. Then, it is put into the honey extractor to separate the honey and keep it for brewing materials. The rest becomes white sugar, which is sent to another room. More than a dozen workers use iron shovels to pile up, shaped like a pile of . Then, from the room below, the white sugar is weighed. The sugar making procedure is completed. Because all are used electric motors, the beets are taken from the east of the factory and made into white sugar at the west end. The procedure is very fast. The beet dregs sent out are provided to the nearby villagers for feeding pigs free of charge. It is said that German sugar factories can turn the dregs into fertilizer.

Business overview

Every ten jins of sugar beets can produce 120 jins to 130 jins of sugar. The cost is about 12 yuan per 100 jins. The current market price is 17 yuan per 100 jins. It is expected that each 100 jins can have a profit of 5 yuan. At the beginning of the product, De Xu Cheng Ji in this city has already underwritten it, and Sanbing is also in contact. Users are happy to eat domestic sugar. The sugar will also pay attention to the sales in the northwest area in the future. There is a great trend of supply exceeding demand. If the factory's machinery is fully powered, it can produce 500 tons of titanium material every day, producing 120,000 jins of sugar, with a value of about 20,000 yuan and a profit of about 6,000 yuan. This year, the raw materials are in short supply, and it is estimated that they are only enough for 20 days. At the beginning of the plan to revive this year, it was believed that if the raw materials could be collected in the predetermined quantity, the sugar making work could last until mid-February next year. After the weather warms up, it is not suitable for sugar making, so alcohol is manufactured instead. Now that the raw materials are not enough for two and a half months, alcohol can only be manufactured in advance to avoid delaying the work. Also, because the machines in the factory only work for half a year each year, it was planned to transport sugar materials (i.e. raw sugar) from the Nanyang area to Jinan for refining and selling everywhere, which would also be profitable. A request was made to the authorities to exempt taxes on transportation, but the result was not approved, so the previous plan was temporarily suspended. (22nd)

Chaoan Seizes Smuggled Goods: Rong Kee's Goods Entirely Confiscated, a Foreign Firm Intervenes to Protect Them

Shantou Correspondence: Smuggled goods from Chao-Shan flood the market, especially peanuts, raw oil, foreign rice, soybeans, and various grains. There are thirty-eight businesses and foreign firms engaged in smuggling. They have formed an association with substantial capital and foreign backing. They have branches and sub-branches in the cities of Chaoan and Jieyang. Smuggled oil, rice, beans, and other goods are transported from other ports to Youtou in large quantities and stored in the Wugiao warehouses. The front of the warehouse has an exit to a tributary of the Han River, making water transportation very convenient. Since these smuggled goods are not subject to agricultural taxes after arriving in Shantou, each load is cheaper than those transported by Chinese merchants. For example, each load of raw oil is more than five yuan cheaper. These smuggled goods arrive from other ports in overwhelming quantities, not only seizing the market share of Chinese merchants but also causing a sharp decline in tax revenue. The authorities are intensifying their efforts to combat smuggling. Fan Zhanpeng, the deputy director of the provincial land and water anti-smuggling bureau, has led anti-smuggling agents and inspectors to Chao-Shan to set up an anti-smuggling network and strictly investigate and crack down. For a time, the atmosphere was quite tense. Countless stalls selling rice and beans were originally located along the roadsides and in the poor residential areas of Shantou. It is said that these were consigned by certain merchants. They earned a commission based on daily sales. Since the strict implementation of anti-smuggling measures, seven or eight out of ten of these rice stalls have disappeared. In addition, rice and beans are piled up like mountains in a certain warehouse in Wugiao, making sales impossible. However, every time a foreign merchant transports smuggled goods inland, he always sends a ruffian to protect them. Sometimes, when the ships carrying smuggled goods pass through villages and towns, they distribute and sell them along the way. As a result, many merchants who are greedy for profit still sell these smuggled goods. For example, Rong Kee in Chaoan City, a large oil mill owner, used to purchase domestic peanuts to extract and sell oil. Recently, he turned to a foreign merchant to purchase large quantities of smuggled peanuts. At the same time, he purchased a small amount of taxable goods from Chinese merchants in Shantou and mixed them in. He also attached stamped tax-paid bags to the goods. Therefore, they always save the bags for future use. This is a clever trick of the merchant. On the 11th of this month, anti-smuggling agents in Chaoan saw porters transporting large quantities of untaxed raw peanuts to Rong Kee. They intercepted the porters and the goods midway. The porters confessed that they were hired by Rong Kee, more than ten in total. For the past ten days or so, they had been transporting goods from a foreign firm to Rong Kee every day, and they only received a small amount of porterage fees. The anti-smuggling branch immediately dispatched a team to arrest several partners of Rong Kee and confiscated all the goods in the shop. The shop owner has fled to a certain place. The partners and laborers of Rong Kee were escorted to Shantou. A certain north-south trading firm in Shantou claimed that Rong Kee had always traded with them and that the proceeds from the goods sold by the firm had not yet been recovered. The surface of the confiscated peanuts was marked with the name of the firm that issued them, and they also held a transfer certificate. The reason why it was not affixed to the bag was a mistake by the boatman. Therefore, they submitted a petition to the Shantou North-South Trading Firm, Grain, and Oil Industry Association, requesting them to forward the petition to the Shantou Anti-Smuggling Director, requesting the return of a portion of the taxed beans to protect the merchants' capital. At the same time, a certain foreign firm in Chaoan also intervened to protect Rong Kee, claiming that Rong Kee's goods were consigned by them. The anti-smuggling bureau believes that this case is of great importance and does not dare to make a decision on the requests of both parties. They have sent an urgent telegram to Guangdong Province to severely punish them. (18th)

Nantong: Langfu Ferry Now Open to Night Navigation

The river surface between Nantong and Changshu is very wide, but there are many hidden shoals, especially the Baimao shoal, which is very dangerous. Vessels traveling to and from must use Langshan in northern Jiangsu and Fushan in southern Jiangsu as landmarks. This section of the river is called Langfu Ferry. In order to facilitate night navigation, the Jianghai Customs has set up light buoys in the waterways around Qingda Reef. From now on, all upstream and downstream vessels can navigate day and night.

Xiaoshan: Bandits Rob Fish Pond at Night

Miaohugang, Qiujiang Township, outside the East Gate of Xiaoshan, is about five li long and has always been used by the Chen family to raise fresh fish, paying donations and taxes every year. Now that the end of the year is approaching, they are planning to catch the fish, but on the night of the 22nd, around the third watch, twenty or thirty strong bandits suddenly arrived, wielding guns and carrying out a large-scale robbery. The bandits fired shots everywhere to show their strength, so the fish farm manager, Du, fled and hid quickly. The bandits captured fish for about two hours before carrying away more than 8,000 catties of fresh fish, shouting as they headed towards Shaoxing. The owner of the pond has already reported to the county government's public security authorities and requested an investigation.

A Brief Explanation of the Structure and Function of the Human Body by Professor Sun Zongpeng of National Central University (Continued)

(VI) The Respiratory System

The function of the respiratory system is to exhale stale air and inhale fresh air to provide the oxygen needed by the body's cells. The nasal cavity and oral cavity are the main passages for breathing, and the lungs are the important organs for breathing. The larynx and trachea communicate with the oral cavity. Inside the larynx is the vocal cord, which is used to produce sound. The larynx and trachea are both composed of cartilage. The trachea runs down the neck from the larynx and divides into two branches to enter the lungs. Each branch divides into countless small branches, and each small branch divides and subdivides until it becomes a small air sac at the end of the branch. The lungs are divided into left and right parts, and each part is further divided into several small chambers. Therefore, the lungs have a spongy shape and can expand and contract. Breathing is carried out by this movement. The two main branches divided from the trachea enter the left and right parts of the lungs respectively. The small air sacs at the ends of the smallest branches are located in the small chambers of the lungs. This is where the inhaled air and the gases in the blood are exchanged. Under normal circumstances, what is exhaled is that, except for the equal amounts of nitrogen exhaled and inhaled, there is more oxygen inhaled and less carbon dioxide, and more carbon dioxide exhaled and less oxygen. Therefore, it is beneficial to breathe more fresh air for the health of the body.

(VII) The Excretory System

The main organs of the excretory system are the kidneys, one on each side, located on the back of the abdominal cavity, on both sides of the spine, in a crescent shape. Each kidney has a tube that connects to the bladder. The structure of the kidney consists of the cortex on the outside and the medulla on the inside. The cortex is filled with Malpighian corpuscles, each of which has a small tube that connects to the medulla. The Malpighian corpuscle is a filter through which blood passes, and the liquid filtered out (urine) flows from the small tube to the medulla and then into the ureter directly to the bladder. The bladder is like a reservoir that, after a certain period of time, releases urine into the urethra and excretes it from the body.

In addition, the excretory organs also include the skin, which excretes sweat and oil in addition to gases. These are all secreted by glands. Tears are also excretory products and come from the lacrimal glands.

(VIII) The Reproductive System

Reproductive organs are divided into male and female. Male reproductive organs include the testes (testicles) and the vas deferens connected to the testes, the seminal vesicles, the prostate gland, and the penis. After sperm mature in the testes, they enter the vas deferens and are transported to the seminal vesicles. At the same time, the body of the vesicle secretes a mucus, which may be used to protect and nourish the sperm. When needed, the sperm is ejected through the penis.

Female reproductive organs include the ovaries and fallopian tubes. The fallopian tubes are not directly connected to the ovaries. After the egg matures, it breaks out of the nest and is pushed into the fallopian tube by the force of the follicular fluid. The lower part of the fallopian tube is called the uterus, and the opening to the outside is called the vagina. After the egg leaves the nest, a yellow spot appears on the ovary, called the corpus luteum, which has the function of internal secretion. If the egg is fertilized, the corpus luteum can inhibit menstruation and maintain the development of the fetus in the uterus, while making the nipples develop for breastfeeding. If the egg has no chance of being fertilized, the corpus luteum gradually degenerates.

(IX) Endocrine Organs

Internal secretion is a special chemical substance secreted by a specific organ and enters the blood to be distributed throughout the body. It can affect the development and physiology of other organs and is very important for the individual's psychological behavior. The organ that secretes this substance is called the endocrine organ, and the substance secreted is called a hormone. In anatomy, little attention is paid to it, but in physiology, it is highly valued. However, physiology is based on anatomy, so a brief description is given below. Anatomically speaking, endocrine organs can be divided into two major categories: ductless glands and duct glands. Ductless glands include the pineal gland, pituitary gland, thyroid gland, parathyroid gland, thymus gland, adrenal gland, and spleen gland. Only the pituitary gland, thyroid gland, parathyroid gland, and adrenal gland have internal secretion functions. The functions of the rest have not yet been proven. Duct endocrine glands include the pancreas (pancreas), liver, and male and female gonads, as well as their appendages. The important ones are briefly described below.

Thyroid Gland: Located below the larynx, on both sides of the trachea, one on each side, connected by a small band-shaped isthmus. Its shape is like a shield, so it is also called the shield-shaped gland. The hormone it secretes contains iodine and greatly affects the development of the body. If this gland is removed or naturally degenerates, the body's development will be incomplete, the hair will fall out, and the skin will be dry. The spirit will be weak and the temperature will be scattered, the movements will be clumsy, the bones will be underdeveloped, the libido will be degenerated, and the intelligence will be underdeveloped, eventually leading to death. If it secretes too much substance, the heartbeat will accelerate, the temperament will be dry, and it will be easily stimulated. In severe cases, there will be symptoms such as protruding eyeballs, enlarged glands, and goiter. This type of disease is generally more common in women than in men and can be treated.

Parathyroid Glands: The parathyroid glands are located within the thyroid gland, one pair on each side, and are quite small and milky white. The hormone they secrete greatly affects the calcification of bones, and its function is like vitamin "D" and ultraviolet rays. If this gland is removed or naturally degenerates, most people cannot survive. In mild cases, the muscles are rigid and cramping. The cartilage disease that occurs in children may be caused by a lack of this hormone, while adults rarely get this disease. If people with this disease are given parathyroid hormone or vitamin "D," they can regain their health, and ultraviolet rays have the same effect.

Adrenal Glands: The adrenal glands are located above the kidneys, hence the name. The inside is divided into two layers, called the cortex and the medulla. The secretions of the two parts are different. The cortex secretes "cortin," and the medulla secretes adrenal essence (this is the old name). Adrenal essence and the sympathetic nervous system have the same origin and have a stimulating effect, stimulating the contraction of smooth muscle and increasing blood pressure. It can also stimulate liver cells to increase the sugar in the liquid, so for those who suffer from diabetes, if too much pancreatic hormone is used, causing the sugar to decrease too much, causing danger, adrenal essence is used to save them. "Cortin" is an essential element for maintaining individual life. If the medulla of the gland is removed, it will not lead to death, but if the cortex is removed, no one can survive. In mild cases, "Addison's disease" will also occur. This gland is also greatly related to the occurrence of other parts of the human body, such as the color of the skin and the development of libido, and it also has a mutually coexisting relationship with other endocrine organs.

Pituitary Gland: The pituitary gland is located below the brain, hence the name. It is divided into three parts: anterior, middle, and posterior. The posterior part is composed of nerve tissue. Scholars in the past paid much attention to the substance it secretes, but according to recent test results, it has no other function except to increase blood pressure and contract smooth muscle. The middle part is located between the anterior and posterior parts, and its function has not yet been proven. Its anterior part is composed of the inner cortex of the mouth and has recently attracted the attention of biologists and physicians. If it is removed, the body will be short and the organs of libido will not develop, but their daily life will be like that of ordinary people. If it secretes too much, the opposite is true. The body will develop more than ordinary people, and the fingers, lips, and nose will be in a special state. Over time, it will become hunchbacked, the movements will be slow, and fatigue will be felt from time to time. There are currently about fourteen types of substances secreted by the anterior part of the pituitary gland, but only a few have been proven by experiments. The most reliable one is the hormone of sex, which can stimulate the development of the ovaries in the female body. Others that are currently being experimented on are the hormone of growth and the hormone of hair growth. No reports have yet been heard on the others.

Pancreas: The pancreas is narrow and long in shape. The middle part is attached to the small intestine, and the anterior and posterior parts float in the intestinal mesentery. In addition to secreting digestive enzymes, its internal secretion substance is pancreatic hormone, called "insulin," which is closely related to sugar metabolism. If it is removed, the liver will lose its function of forming liver powder, and the sugar in the blood will increase, resulting in diabetes. Therefore, pancreatic hormone is used to treat diabetes and is quite effective, and it has the same function as adrenal essence.

Gonads: Gonads are divided into two types, male and female. Male glands secrete male hormones to stimulate male organs and secondary sexual characteristics. If they are removed, men will be in a female state, with gentle emotions, sharp voices, and no testicles. The so-called theory of sexual inversion is due to this. If the elderly are weak, it can be said that they are rejuvenating.

The organs that secrete female hormones are the ovaries and placenta, etc. Female hormones have the function of stimulating the development of the ovaries and eggs, and regulating menstruation. As mentioned above, the sexual hormones of the pituitary gland and the hormones of the corpus luteum stimulate the development of the breast and maintain the fetus by stopping menstruation.

Liver: The liver is located in the upper part of the abdominal cavity and is the largest of the glands. In addition to performing digestive functions, it is closely related to anemia. People with anemia can increase hemoglobin and red blood cells by eating liver or liver essence. For this reason, it is also classified as an endocrine organ.

The scope of endocrinology is extremely large and extremely complex, and further efforts are needed to advance it. (The End)

Over Two Thousand Students Petition in the Capital, Departing from the North Station Yesterday, Leaving at 5 PM, Stopped at Qingyang Port, Telegraphed Lin and Chiang for Permission, Chiang Advised Students to Return to School, University President Resigned, Partial Martial Law in the City

The Fudan University students and others who formed a petition delegation to the capital arrived at the North Station the day before yesterday. They planned to take a train to the capital to petition, but the railway bureau did not allow the train to depart, resulting in a stalemate. The petitioning students remained on the first and second platforms. Yesterday morning, over one thousand students from Tongji University, Southeast Medical College, Jianguo Middle School, Zhengfeng Middle School, Guanghua Middle School, Daxia University, Shibei Middle School, and Huanghuagang Middle School, and more than ten other schools, marched in formation to the North Station to participate. The total number of people was estimated to be over two thousand. However, the railway bureau only agreed to transport the petitioning students to the capital at 5:20 PM. A large number of armed security teams accompanied the train to maintain order. It was reported that when the train arrived at Qingyang Port Station, all students were persuaded to get off the train and were escorted back to Shanghai by the security team.
