Central Government's Comfort Has No Effect

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that after receiving a telegram from Mayor Wu reporting the Fudan student petition, Premier Chiang of the Executive Yuan replied by telegram the day before yesterday at midnight, ordering Fudan University President Li Denghui to offer comfort and persuade them to return, with extremely tactful wording. After consulting with the authorities, President Li, along with Secretary-General Yu Tongyin and Director of the Education Department Zhang Yousan, took the telegram, had the transcribed telegram posted on the carriages, and went to each of the carriages where the students were staying to explain in detail and urge them to return to school, informing them that Premier Chiang's telegram reply was extremely satisfactory, that the student petition had come to a result, and that they should not waste their studies, urging them to all return to school. While speaking, tears welled up in his eyes. The students were quite moved and shouted slogans in support of President Li, asking President Li to return to school. Seeing that things had come to this point, Li and Secretary-General Jin and others took a car back to the school to discuss the aftermath.

Li Denghui Angrily Submits His Resignation

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that Fudan University President Li Denghui, after failing to persuade the students the night before last at about 12 o'clock, returned to the school and said to a Xin Sheng News Agency reporter at the North Station, "Fudan has a long history of ten years, and its alumni are all over the country. I have devoted my life to Fudan's affairs. I love the country, but I also love Fudan. To save the country, there must be a whole plan before it can be gradually realized. Now, the students of Fudan do not listen to persuasion and rashly insist on going to the capital to petition, I am afraid that it will be difficult to have results. Therefore, I have repeatedly persuaded them and sincerely met with all the students, but there was no response. Fudan is my second life. I cannot bear to see the students waste their studies and squander their time. I cannot be responsible for this kind of extraordinary action and the future situation. Therefore, I decided to resign immediately and abandon all responsibilities of Fudan's affairs to promote the students' final awakening." Yesterday afternoon, a notice was issued, which stated, "This school's students, driven by patriotic enthusiasm, gathered several hundred people at the North Station on the morning of the 23rd to prepare to go to the capital to petition. However, because the train could not depart, the students were stranded at the station and insisted resolutely. I personally went to the station to persuade them to return to school, but it had no effect. Later in the evening, I received a telegram from Premier Chiang, expressing his willingness to accept the opinions of the students of this school. It was my intention that the students' purpose of going to the capital was simply to express public opinion and contribute opinions. Now that Premier Chiang has telegraphed his acceptance, the students really have no need to go to the capital again. Therefore, I took the telegram to the station and made a final effort to persuade the students, and read Premier Chiang's telegram to the public in each carriage, intending that the students would accept this reply as satisfactory. Who knew that after guiding them for a long time, there was no result. The students' persistence remained the same, and they turned a deaf ear to my words. I have been serving this school for thirty years, and when this major event occurred, I could not lead the students to be convinced, which shows that my usual virtues have not been trusted and my training has been ineffective. I feel deeply guilty. Therefore, from today, I have decided to resign. In addition to having requested the school board to hire a successor, I hereby announce this. Li Denghui." Upon hearing the news, the Fudan Alumni Association believed that Li had presided over the alma mater for many years and his merits were all there, so how could they allow him to retreat? They immediately appointed Xi Yushu and Ye Bingfu as representatives to earnestly persuade President Li to stay.

The students of the school immediately left the station, lined up and returned to school, shouting slogans in support of the Central Government along the way.

Final Solution: Decision to Depart by Train

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that at 4:30 PM yesterday, the municipal authorities decided to approve the students' request and ordered the station to depart by train to allow the students to go to Beijing to petition. At 4:40 PM, Director Cai Jinjun of the Public Security Bureau directed more than two hundred police officers, each holding bamboo poles, to spread out on the two platforms of the North Station, cutting off traffic on one side and broadcasting announcements on the North Station platform, telling the petitioning students in each car that the train was now determined to go to Nanjing, and that those who were willing could get on the train quickly, and those who were unwilling could get off the train and be escorted back to school by the security team, but they should not stop on the platform to avoid accidents. After twenty minutes of deployment, at 5:10 PM, each car officially departed. The two thousand petitioning students in the car were able to comply with the authorities' advice and got on the car one after another to petition in Beijing. When the train departed, they shouted slogans such as "Save the country and ask for advice". At the same time, there were large white cloth banners at the entrances of each platform in the station, which read: "Everyone pay attention, don't give the enemy a chance," "People who are really working hard to save the country should beware of the activities of thugs," and "Maintain the patriotic movement and strictly arrest the rioters."

The City Government Dispersed the Students: The Process

Central News Agency reports that the students of major middle and high schools in this city recently petitioned the municipal government in batches. Because the municipal government believed that their motives were initially pure and their patriotism was sincere, Mayor Wu met them openly and agreed to forward the various petitions to the Central Government. However, since the day before yesterday (25th) at noon, three hundred students from a part of Fudan University went to the North Station to take a train to Beijing to petition, the situation has gradually become serious. The Party and government authorities, in addition to sending personnel to various schools to dissuade other students from agreeing, have also repeatedly sent personnel to the North Station to persuade them to return to school, but to no effect. Later, Mayor Wu telegraphed Premier Chiang to ask for instructions. That night, Premier Chiang sent a reply telegram to Fudan University President Li, urging the students to return to school, with unusually sincere wording. However, the students were still not aware and stayed at the station and refused to leave, and beat several unarmed police officers who gave them well-intentioned advice, and distributed reactionary leaflets. Yesterday morning, a part of middle school students, who were very young, were used by others and gathered in the Continental Commercial Building on Nanjing Road, attempting to parade in the concession, and the leaflets they distributed also had a lot of reactionary colors. According to investigations, members of the Communist Party and the Social Democratic Party were directing and manipulating behind the scenes. Their plan was to use the students who were giving speeches to disrupt the autumn order in this city, block traffic in various places, and prepare to create a tragic case that could expand the storm, and even conspired to instigate a rush into the concession to create international disputes and increase the government's difficulties in dealing with it. The municipal government and the garrison headquarters, aware of this, must not allow the reactionary elements to take the opportunity to cause trouble, and for the sake of protecting young students, they notified the principals of various universities to go to the station at 2 PM to urge the students to return to school. Except for students from a few schools such as Chizhi University who followed the request to return to school, a part of the students from Fudan, Tongji, Jianguo Middle School, and Shibei Middle School, numbering several hundred, stayed at the station. However, the North Station was adjacent to the concession, and the crisis was latent, so an order was issued to equip locomotives to transport all these students to the suburbs and forcibly disband them. It is reported that the principals of various universities, in addition to urging the students who stayed at the school to follow Premier Chiang's order and send representatives to Beijing on the 15th of next month, do not need to petition again at this time, and will also send personnel to the suburbs to persuade the students of their respective schools to return to school. As for the middle schools, it is reported that the Municipal Education Bureau has received an order from the municipal government to inform all public and private middle schools in the city to start their winter vacation early from today, and parents are responsible for taking their students back to avoid being coerced and accidents. It is said that all middle schools will comply with this order today.

Arriving at Biaoyang Port, Various Schools Picked Them Up

Shanghai News Agency reports that after the train left the North Station, it was reported that it arrived at Qingyang Port Station at 6:30 PM and stopped. Security teams and others also took two other trains to maintain order. The authorities of various universities rushed to persuade the students and prepared large cars to pick up the students of various schools separately.

Partial Martial Law Declared in the City

Central News Agency reports that the Songhu Garrison Headquarters and the Shanghai Municipal Government issued a notice yesterday, which stated, "Notice: Student movements are originally patriotic and enthusiastic. Therefore, in recent days, the government authorities have been doing their best to maintain local order while seeking to protect young people. However, today, it was discovered that there are actually Communist Party members and other reactionary elements who are taking advantage of the student movement to carry out their plots of causing trouble and brewing disasters. The situation in this city is complicated. If we do not take strict precautions, accidents may occur at any time. In order to maintain the public security and local order of the city, we hereby announce partial martial law. In addition to issuing orders separately, we must immediately inform the public. This notice is hereby issued. Wu Tiecheng, Mayor of Shanghai and Commander of the Songhu Garrison, December 24, 24th year of the Republic of China."

Various Middle Schools Started Vacation Early

Central News Agency reports that after the authorities earnestly persuaded and openly explained the patriotic movement of students in major middle and high schools in the city in recent days, they have all expressed their satisfaction and are studying as usual. However, yesterday, the authorities investigated and found that trouble makers mixed into the student ranks at the North Railway Station on Nanjing Road and the Zhabei Oriental Library, posing as students and distributing reactionary leaflets and slogans, plotting wrongdoing. The general young students, therefore, decided that the patriotic movement was originally out of a sacred patriotic psychology and would never be used by anyone. They were deeply afraid of being deceived by reactionary elements, so they automatically withdrew. The authorities are investigating the trouble makers who are trying to use the students to plot wrongdoing, and the Education Bureau of the car has ordered all middle schools in the city to start their vacation early and to inform the parents of each student to go to the school to pick them up to avoid being coerced and accidents. The authorities of various universities are now also studying effective measures to prevent any actions by reactionary elements.

The Boundary Road of Clone was Once Disturbed

The Public Concession Huishi Police Department, because the Boundary Road is only separated from this station by an iron fence, was deeply afraid of accidents, so the district chief Kang Chou dispatched the Huashi detectives Shang Wu and Tao Genrong, the Huabu head Xu Zhengqin, etc. to patrol the boundary road with Western detectives to maintain order. Fearing that the police force was insufficient, they transferred the reserve team members to patrol back and forth in two police cars. At 11:50 AM yesterday morning, two or three hundred students from Tongji University suddenly came out of the North Station to the Boundary Road, lined up and shouted slogans, planning to go to Clone Road and other places. The police officers closed the iron gate at the intersection of Clone Road and Boundary Road to prevent them from advancing, and the two police cars also rushed to the scene at this time. Later, senior police officers persuaded the students to obey the order and avoid accidents. The students also negotiated with the police through representatives for a long time, but there was no result. The representative then led all the students back to the North Station, and the situation calmed down.

Distributing Leaflets on Nanjing Road

Central News Agency reports that at about 8 AM yesterday morning, about two hundred male and female students gathered at the Nanjing Road Ball Field, preparing to distribute leaflets. The Laozha Police Department and the Central Police Department received the news and prepared cars to intercept the Chinese and Western detectives to disperse them. A part of the students retreated to the nearby Continental Commercial Building and Shandong Road, Henan Road and other places. In the chaos, there were slight conflicts with each other. The Central Police Department and the Laozha Police Department captured eight students, a part of whom had been released earlier. The students were all wearing casual clothes. At about 9 AM, the students had completely dispersed and returned to normal. The leaflets and slogans left on the road were also cleared by the cleaners sent by the police department.

According to our newspaper's investigation, at 8:30 AM yesterday morning, the Central Police Department of the Public Concession suddenly received a secret report saying that a large number of students would go to Nanjing Road to distribute leaflets and give open-air speeches. After receiving the report, the police authorities were deeply afraid that the large number of people would affect public security, so they immediately selected Chinese and Western police chiefs to supervise a large team of detectives to rush to Nanjing Road to patrol and suppress them. They found no less than five or six hundred students and civilians gathered near the Continental Commercial Building at the intersection of Shandong Road. The students were distributing leaflets to the public. The police chiefs and others persuaded them tactfully, hoping that the public would disperse, but the persuaders despised them, so they immediately chased them away, and a conflict occurred. The Western police chief Hua Sheng was injured in the face, Feinas was injured in the arms and face, and in addition to Wei Situo's injuries on his face, his hat was also broken. Only Dong Chongxiang of Marilyn College was arrested on the spot. In addition, Zheng Shuwei, who was doing business at the exchange, was also arrested. Until 11 AM, the order at that place returned to normal. The arrested Dong and Zheng were sent to the First Special District Local Court at 12:30 PM and interrogated by Judge Dai Rongduo in the Second Court. The lawyer of the Bureau of Public Works prosecuted Dong and Zheng for obstructing official duties in violation of Articles 135 and 136 of the Criminal Law. The three Western police chiefs, Hua Sheng, Feinas, and Wei Situo, successively went to court to state the circumstances of the incident. Judge Dai then interrogated the two defendants, Dong and Zheng, and immediately announced the verdict in court, sentencing each to three months in prison, suspended for three years. During the appeal period, they should each pay a shop guarantee that they would be available on call. After the verdict, the police transferred the two to the bail office, and they could be free as soon as the bail formalities were completed. However, Zheng Shuwei seemed to have been slightly injured in the head during the conflict, so his head was wrapped in white cloth.

Students Parade in Nanshi and Zhabei

Xin Xin News Agency reports that yesterday morning, students from Qingxin Middle School, Minli Middle School, Minli Girls' Middle School, Shanghai Girls' Middle School, Wuben Girls' Middle School, and Datong Attached Middle School in Nanshi responded to the students of Fudan University's request to go to Beijing to petition, and set off in teams from the school to parade and demonstrate along Zhonghua Road, Laoximen, Fangxie Road, and Chezhan Road, shouting patriotic slogans and distributing various leaflets along the way. In Zhabei, students from Aiguo Girls' Middle School, Yuqing Middle School, Liangjiang Women's Physical Education Teachers' College, Business College, Chizhi, and other schools gathered in teams on Jiangwan Road, Baoshan Road, and Datong Road, and paraded along Beisichuan Road in the concession. They also shouted slogans and distributed leaflets along the way. The order was still good, and fortunately no accidents occurred.

Representatives from All Circles Were Sent to Comfort the Students

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that from 10 PM the night before last to yesterday afternoon, the visitors from all walks of life to the North Station to comfort the students were endless. The schools included Datong, Chizhi, Daxia, Jinan, Jiaotong, Sino-French, China, Guanghua, and Shanghai Universities, Jianguo Middle School, Fudan Experimental Middle School, etc. The Fudan students who stayed at the school also sent more than thirty representatives yesterday morning, carrying bread and other comfort items, to the station to comfort the Fudan Alumni Association, which is a powerful organization of graduates of the school, and yesterday afternoon also sent representatives Ye Bingfu, Xi Yushu, Liu Bainian, Wang Sifang, and others to the station to comfort them, and urged them to go to school. In addition to the City Federation, there was also the National Products Manufacturers Association, which donated a large number of food products from various food companies to transport them to comfort the students. The National Postal Workers' Union and the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union sent representatives Lu Jingtu and others to sell dry food and fruit. All colleagues of Shanghai Zhengzhong Bookstore organized the "Zhengzhong Bookstore Shanghai Colleagues Save the Country Association" to implement the work of assisting students petitioning in Beijing, and raised 18 yuan on the spot, and appointed Song Jinren and others as representatives to purchase food and comfort them at the North Station. It was also reported that at about 5 PM yesterday afternoon, former Central Committee member He Xiangning also went to the station in her private capacity to comfort the students she knew well and encourage their patriotic movement. He's old and frail appearance attracted much attention.

In addition, the people of Zhonghua Jieyun Company opposite the North Station witnessed the students camping overnight at the station and specially bought a large basket of bread to send to them yesterday, and sent a letter saying, "Dear Sir/Madam, the colleagues of our company express our deep sympathy for your patriotic enthusiasm, and specially prepare a few snacks to relieve your hunger for camping overnight at the station and express our condolences. We wish you all to win glory for the Chinese nation."

This City's Fourteen Legal Organizations Express Their Views on the Current Situation; Jointly Send a Telegram to the Central Government Offering Suggestions and a Separate Telegram Urging Song Zheyuan

Fourteen legal organizations in this city, including the Lawyers Association, the National Federation of Commerce, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, and the Journalists Association, believing that the situation in North China is severe and the nation's survival has reached a critical juncture, jointly sent telegrams to various departments of the Central Government yesterday, opposing the Hebei-Chahar autonomy, urging the swift suppression of rebels, and safeguarding legitimate patriotic movements. They also sent a separate telegram urging Song Zheyuan and expressing sympathy to the students in Peiping. The telegrams are transcribed below:

Telegram to the Central Government, the Executive Committee of the Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, Chairman Lin of the National Government, Premier Jiang of the Executive Yuan, and Minister Zhang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs: Since the September 18th Incident, four years have passed. All of our people have endured pain and tears, understanding the government's difficult situation and hoping for self-reliance and revitalization. Self-reliance should mean safeguarding our unlost sovereignty and territory. If sovereignty is further divided and territory further trampled, it means watching the continuation of self-reliance be destroyed. Not only will limited sovereignty and territory fail to satisfy insatiable desires, but the content of self-reliance will also become weaker. If this is the case, how can we speak of self-reliance? Therefore, the current plan should be to swiftly punish those who harm the country and rebel, resolutely stop the Hebei-Chahar autonomy, and vigorously protect legitimate patriotic movements, so that treacherous elements dare not follow suit, and national strength will not be divided. Otherwise, those who follow the enemy will receive invisible rewards, and patriots will suffer tangible punishments. With rewards and punishments reversed, even if the government has no intention of harming the country, how can it defend against the fault of harming the country? The undersigned public organizations, with a sense of walking on thin ice and standing on the edge of a cliff, fulfill the responsibility of every citizen for the nation's rise and fall, and speak frankly. We hope you will listen attentively. (Signed: Shanghai Lawyers Association, National Federation of Commerce, Municipal Education Association, Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, Certified Public Accountants Association, Journalists Association, Municipal Farmers Association, Joint Association of Citizens of Special District One, Joint Association of Citizens of Special District Two, National Federation of New Pharmaceutical Industry, China Labor Association, National Postal Workers Union, China National Products Manufacturers Federation, Teachers Federation of Secondary Schools)

Telegram to Song Zheyuan, Chairman Song of the Hebei Provincial Government: Since the battles of Xifengkou and Shalukou, your name has resonated both domestically and internationally, adding glory to the history of national humiliation. This is why the people of the country have placed their hearts on you, hoping that you can do more in the future. But now, news reports indicate that you have shifted the blade of loyalty and bravery from Shalukou to the patriotic students. In that case, the commendable merits of defending the territory in the past will not only lose their value, but people may also suspect that you are using them as a tool for seeking personal glory. Whether to leave a good or bad name is your own choice, and there is no need for others to worry needlessly. However, out of love for you, we dare not remain silent. We sincerely hope that you will carefully consider history, punish the wicked, and clarify your ambitions, so as to comfort the hearts of those who love you and appease the anger and grief of the world. This would be most fortunate. (Signed as above)

Message of Sympathy to the Students Addressed to all students of Peking University, Yenching University, Peiping University, Chaoyang University, Tsinghua University, Fu Jen Catholic University, and the Peiping Normal University: Since the national crisis, the people of the country have understood the government's difficult situation, enduring pain and tears, waiting for self-improvement after enduring hardship. Now, four years have passed. You, compelled by accumulated grievances, are not afraid of blades and spears, using the sincerity of bare-handed entreaties to safeguard the integrity of the territory and sovereignty. Your hearts are extremely sincere, and your spirit is extremely strong. Upon hearing of this from afar, everyone is inspired. In addition to sending telegrams to the central government officials and Chairman Song of Hebei Province, we hereby express our sympathy. We hope that you will uphold your patriotic and fearless spirit, and strive for self-defense. We, though lacking in ability, pledge to be your strong backing. (Signed as above)

Newly Appointed Ambassador to Germany, Cheng Tianfang, Departed Yesterday; He Published a Letter to the German People Before His Departure

The newly appointed Ambassador to Germany, Mr. Cheng Tianfang, took the Jinghui ferry across the river from the Xinguanshi Wharf at 2:30 PM yesterday and boarded the Prussode Wheel of the North German Company. He set sail for his post abroad at around 4:00 PM. Those who came to see him off included Mr. Geng Jiaqi, representing Mayor Wu, Chairman Xu Shiying of the Disaster Relief Committee, Director Zhou Jue of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Deputy Director Zhao Tiezhang, Huang Yanpei, Wang Yunwu, the consuls of Germany and Austria in Shanghai, and many of Mr. Cheng's relatives and friends. Those who traveled with him included Embassy Secretary Qiu Changkang, Attaché Chen Zehua, and Clerk Mao Biping. Mr. Cheng's family will travel to Germany next spring. Mr. Strewe, the editor-in-chief of the German newspaper Deutsche Allgeine Zeitung, has worked in China for many years, has extensive knowledge of Chinese culture, and has always expressed sympathy for the Chinese nation. He often publishes articles in the newspaper praising China and upholding justice. In 1930, the German industrial inspection team that came to China was initiated by Mr. Strewe. He recently came to China for a visit and met with Mr. Cheng Tianfang, our country's first ambassador to Germany, in Beijing. They had a very pleasant conversation. Mr. Strewe specially requested Ambassador Cheng to write a short article on the day of his departure, which he would telegraph to Germany for publication in German newspapers. Mr. Cheng agreed to his request. The translated manuscript of the article is published below: Today is the eve of Christmas, and I am also departing for Germany today. At the request of Mr. Strewe, I respectfully address a few words to the German people as a Christmas gift. When I was a child, I knew that there was a German nation in the world, whose people were fond of learning and deep in thought, persevering and resolute. Therefore, their achievements in science, philosophy, engineering, industry, medicine, and art are admired and praised by the whole world. The rapid development of the German Empire was unprecedented in the history of the world. At that time, I was eager to set foot in Germany and see the facilities of this great nation. This wish has been cherished for twenty-five years, and today I am able to fulfill this hope as the first ambassador to Germany, which is the most honorable and joyful thing for me. After the Great War, Germany was in the most difficult and painful environment, but with the efforts and struggles of the German government and people, they overcame the environment and revived. China is also encountering an extremely difficult and painful environment. In the midst of our efforts and struggles, every time we think of the example of Germany's revival, we gain infinite courage. China and Germany have always had friendly relations. In recent years, the cooperation between the two countries in culture and economic development has been increasing, which will allow the people of the two countries to understand each other better and become more friendly. Jesus said, "Do unto others as you would have them do unto you." Confucius also said, "Help others establish themselves, help others succeed." The teachings of Chinese and Western sages are the same. If the two great nations of China and Germany follow this spirit and engage in mutual assistance, they will make a great contribution to the world. I, Cheng Tianfang, am willing to do my best to contribute to this. Cheng Tianfang.

Those who accompanied Ambassador Cheng yesterday included Embassy Secretary Qiu Changkang, Attaché Chen Zehua, Clerk Mao Baoping, and Zhu Jianmin, Zhou Chixia, Xiao Zuoliang, and Si Songxi, graduates of the Department of Diplomacy of the Central Political School who went to Germany for internships, and a servant, a total of eight people. Embassy Secretary Li Weiguo in September and Yao Dingchen in November had already gone to Germany to arrange everything. As for Ambassador Cheng's wife and children, they will stay in China temporarily due to some matters and will go there next spring.

Ambassador Cheng (second from left) with well-wishers (photo by Zhu Shunlin)

The Loan Investigation Committee Approved Loans of Over 38,000 Yuan; Requested Funds to Promote Acceptance Bills and Submitted it to the Ministry of Finance for Review

The Shanghai Industry and Commerce Loan Committee held its 19th meeting at the China National Products Bank at 4:00 PM on the 23rd. The committee members present were Cai Zengji, Qin Runqing, Yu Zuoting (representing Qin Runqing), Chen Guangfu, Wang Xiaolai, Bei Songsun, Du Yuesheng (representing Wang Xiaolai), Song Ziliang, Xi Demao, Zhang Peishen, etc., chaired by Cai Zengji. After reporting on the routine work, seven applications for credit small loans were submitted. After careful review, it was decided that loans would be granted to two companies as requested, loans would be granted at half the requested amount to twenty-one companies, and loans would be granted with a partial reduction to thirty companies, totaling 38,150 yuan in loans approved. In addition, seventeen companies were rejected for loans, either because their business did not conform to the loan principles, or because the use of the loan did not comply with the regulations, or because they lacked the required qualifications. The committee will notify the original applicants of the approved cases. In addition, members of the Noodle and Shoe Leather Nail Industry Associations have borrowed small amounts of less than 100 yuan from the Loan Committee, with joint guarantees from three companies in the same industry. Now, many companies in these industries who did not participate in the first loan application have requested the Industry Association to ask the Loan Committee to follow the previous example and approve small loans. After discussion, the committee decided to approve the application for loans according to the previous example. It is heard that the committee is still continuing to handle industrial and commercial credit loans. Companies in need of loans can obtain application forms and inquire about procedures at the committee's office on the second floor of the China National Products Bank on Tianjin Road. In addition, regarding the ten cases of promoting acceptance bills, the committee gathered opinions from all parties, submitted them for reconsideration, and decided to submit all the opinions to the Ministry of Finance for review.

After finishing his business, he came to Shanghai to visit various national product factories. Mr. Lu believed that in recent years, the roads in Yunnan Province have developed and the consumption of gasoline has increased significantly. Moreover, the high freight costs are greatly hindering the future of the highway business. He had long heard that the wood charcoal-fueled oil substitute stove invented by Tang Zhongming of Henan had been adopted by many provincial highways. He took advantage of his trip to Shanghai to visit the Zhongming Factory on Qiqihar Road in Yangshupu yesterday. He was received by Fan Zhengbo, Chairman of the factory, Tang Yunqing, General Manager, and Tang Zhongming, Director of the factory. Mr. Lu was very satisfied with the factory's products and purchased twenty Zhongming-style charcoal-fueled oil substitute stoves in the name of the Yunnan Provincial Highway Administration for trial use in Yunnan. Yesterday afternoon, he officially signed the contract at the Fu Dian Bank and planned to set up branch factories in Yunnan and Guizhou provinces to manufacture in large quantities. Mr. Lu, having completed his business, is scheduled to go to Hong Kong and then to Yunnan tomorrow.

The Land Bureau Plans to Formulate Provisional Measures for Land Mortgage Rights; The Executive Yuan Orders Revisions to be Submitted for Review; The Judicial Yuan Must Reinterpret

The Shanghai Land Bureau previously explained that according to Interpretation No. 493 of the Judicial Yuan, the auction of collateral must be implemented after a court ruling is finalized. Therefore, mortgages are stagnant, which hinders the flow of funds. After Director Cai examined the social situation, he drafted nine articles of the Provisional Measures for Implementing Land License Mortgage Rights in Shanghai and submitted them to the municipal government for submission to the Executive Yuan for instructions. Regarding the creditor's application to auction rental guarantee objects, there is no need for a final judgment as an enforcement title, and it should be approved for auction. The Judicial Administration Department issued Order No. 2221 to its subordinate courts for compliance on June 30, 23rd. The Judicial Yuan's Interpretation No. 492 is currently being requested by the Executive Yuan for reinterpretation. The Land License Mortgage Rights Provisional Measures are now being revised in accordance with the regulations. It is learned that the original text of Instruction No. 16659 of the Municipal Government is as follows: A case was received from the Executive Yuan's Instruction No. 3731, which stated: A submission of No. 493 on November 20, 24th, was submitted for the drafting of provisional measures for the implementation of land license mortgage rights in Shanghai, please review and order compliance. The submitted and attached documents have been fully understood. The proposed draft provisional measures for the implementation of land pledge rights in Shanghai contradicts the provisions of the Civil Code and should not be approved. It has been investigated that a creditor's application to auction collateral does not require a final judgment as an enforcement title, and it should be approved for auction. The Judicial Administration Department issued Instruction No. 2221 to the Jiangsu Higher Court and forwarded it to its subordinate courts for compliance on June 30, 23rd. In addition, the Municipal Council of Shanghai and others requested the Judicial Yuan to reinterpret Court Order No. 93 and requested the Legislative Yuan to promulgate the Registration Law and Auction Law as soon as possible to encourage real estate circulation and to provide relief to industry and commerce. It is necessary to revise and resubmit the report in accordance with the law for review and transfer. This order, etc., because of the previous instructions, should be reported to the Bureau for compliance and reported for review and transfer.

The report briefly stated that today, all the gentlemen from the city's Chinese, Western, vegetarian, and restaurant industries are invited to discuss the implementation of the aviation patriotic donation fundraising. Director-General Wu and Secretary-General Li were unable to attend due to other commitments and are represented by their brothers. The first fundraising campaign in the city was met with enthusiastic support from people from all walks of life, with over one hundred thousand members recruited. The fundraising of aviation patriotic donations from various industries, including the hotel industry, fresh meat industry, and fresh pork vending industry, has achieved excellent results. The fourth meeting of the Board of Directors of the China Aviation Association this year resolved to continue the second micro-fundraising campaign. Since its commencement in March, it has relied on the enthusiastic promotion of the captains and has achieved excellent results. Fundraising for aviation patriotic donations from the freight vehicle industry, brick and tile transportation industry, sand and gravel industry, yellow sand crushed stone industry, and dance hall industry has also been carried out, with details published repeatedly. Gentlemen in your industry have always been willing to support the patriotic cause, so it is also being organized. Aviation patriotic donations will be collected according to the standard of business income. Ten methods have been formulated and please express your opinions as much as possible and determine the commencement date, etc. Subsequently, representatives such as Li Mancun from Xing Hua Lou and Lao Zheng Long spoke one after another, stating that the collection of aviation patriotic donations in this industry is to support the aviation patriotic movement, and we should strive to carry it out to fulfill our national duty. It was discussed and decided that the official collection would commence on January 15, 1936, and the ten methods were approved. The original methods are as follows: Shanghai Restaurant Industry Collection of Aviation Patriotic Donation Methods: The China Aviation Association formulates these methods to widely raise aviation patriotic funds. All restaurant industries, regardless of Chinese, Western, meat, vegetarian, banquets, or snacks, are subject to collection. For all restaurant industries, the aviation patriotic donation collection is at a rate of one percent (for example, one cent is collected for every dollar spent). Increases progressively above one dollar and is waived below one dollar. Regardless of whether customers pay cash or charge for food and beverages, the aforementioned donation must be paid in cash. The collection of aviation patriotic donations for the restaurant industry is limited to 100,000 yuan. All restaurant industries must post the aviation patriotic donation collection notice and methods in the dining room or restaurant for customers to read. All aviation patriotic donations collected by the restaurant industry must be recorded on the triplicate receipt issued by the China Aviation Association, with the first copy given to the customer. The aviation patriotic donations collected by the restaurant industry shall be settled every half month and submitted to the General Captain's Office of the Shanghai Fundraising Team of the China Aviation Association. After the commencement of the aviation patriotic donation collection in the restaurant industry, the China Aviation Association may dispatch personnel to inspect the collection situation at any time. If there is any fraud, it shall be reported to the government for disposition in accordance with the law. The China Aviation Association shall announce the amount of aviation patriotic donations collected by the restaurant industry every month. These methods shall be submitted to the government for approval and implementation.

City Chamber of Commerce Instructions: Doubts About Sticking Stamps

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce responded to Shen Yuanlai & Co. yesterday regarding doubts about sticking stamps, stating: Your letter of the 23rd of this month was received, listing four points of doubt regarding stamp tax, requesting instructions, etc. The answers are as follows: (1) A note requesting payment of money or goods, if it cannot be used as a voucher for withdrawing money or goods independently, does not need to be stamped. (2) All receipts (original and duplicate) used by various industries to settle accounts shall be stamped according to the amount: one cent for amounts of three yuan or more, two cents for amounts of ten yuan or more, and three cents for amounts of one hundred yuan or more, to be affixed by the receiver. If the number of stamps is insufficient, the receiver shall be responsible. The duplicate may be exempt from stamping. (3) For the Municipal Council's rent book, if the first page contains the landlord's and tenant's rent, a stamp of two cents shall be affixed to each piece in accordance with the lease contract. For blank rent tickets listed in the book, each piece shall be stamped with two cents in accordance with the example of the rent receipt before use or payment. (4) For submission of money by introduction note, the receiver shall affix the stamps in accordance with the law.

Lu Shaotang's Embezzlement Conviction: Sentenced to One and a Half Years, Suspended for Two Years

Lu Shaotang, the general manager of the Suzhou branch of the Bank of Communications and a prominent real estate businessman, was jointly charged with his son, Bingsheng, for embezzling 239,000 yuan in banknotes from the bank. After the incident, Shaotang fled, and Bingsheng was arrested and sentenced by the First Special District Court to one year and six months in prison. However, Bingsheng was dissatisfied and is still appealing the first instance. Shaotang recently repaid the debt, and the bank authorities agreed not to pursue the matter. Therefore, he surrendered himself to the police station a few days ago and was brought to court for investigation. He was ordered to be released on bail. Yesterday morning, the date for sentencing, Lu surrendered himself again. Judge Feng Shide opened the court and announced the judgment: Lu Shaotang was sentenced to one year and six months in prison for embezzlement, suspended for two years.

Appeal Returned for Retrial: Ren Sida and Others Not Guilty; Buying and Selling Public Bonds Did Not Harm the National Treasury; Money Obtained from Purchasing Land Was Commission

Ren Sida, the former manager of the Shanghai branch of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, was implicated when Liu Shufan, the director of the Savings and Remittance Bureau, was impeached. Later, he and Liu were prosecuted by the prosecutor. The First Special District Court sentenced them to imprisonment. Liu was acquitted in the second instance, while Ren and Zhao Binshan, the real estate broker who was also sentenced to imprisonment in the same case, appealed to the Supreme Court. After review, the court found that there were still doubts and returned the case to the Second Branch of the High Court for retrial. Recently, Judge Yu questioned Ren and Zhao. It was found that Ren, while serving as manager of the Savings and Remittance Bureau, handled the buying and selling of public bonds for Xun Ji and did not harm the national treasury. Zhao Binshan, when Yang Jianping was the director of the Savings and Remittance Bureau, introduced the bureau to purchase land, and the money obtained was actually commission. Yesterday afternoon, the court reopened and announced the judgment: the original judgment was overturned, and Ren Sida and Zhao Binshan were declared not guilty. The prosecutor's appeal was rejected, and the plaintiff's incidental civil suit was dismissed.

Counselor of the British Embassy in Tokyo Commits Suicide En Route; Suicide Due to Suffering from Illness; Body Discharged Upon Arrival in Shanghai

Mr. Derrer, the counselor of the British Embassy in Tokyo, recently took a vacation to Manila and returned to his post on the President McKinley. He committed suicide with a gun on board. His body has been unloaded in Shanghai. Yesterday morning, Coroner Haines from the British Consulate General examined the remains and ruled that the death was due to temporary mental derangement caused by suffering from illness. Derrer had just taken office from Washington on October 9th of this year. His wife and children are currently residing in England.

Xu Jujin, an accountant at the Accounting Office of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureau, was carrying over 4,200 yuan in legal tender to the Engineering Office to pay salaries at 2:30 PM on the 23rd. Xu managed to free himself and reported to the police station, requesting investigation. He was taken back to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special District Court, where Judge Jiang Shuzi interrogated him. According to news from the Railway Bureau, Xu Jujin, a disbursing officer at the Accounting Office of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, was carrying money to the Engineering Office to pay December salaries at 2:30 PM on the 23rd of this month when he was suddenly bound hand and foot by two robbers, who stole over 4,200 yuan in cash. Assault on Tram Conductor; Caused by Argument Over Forcing Purchase of Tickets; Conductor Mu Xiaoshan Severely Beaten; - The Troublemaking Members Have Been Sent to Court -

Chen Huaxiang (24 years old, local, residing at No. 40 Luban Road, Huajie, works as an automobile coppersmith) and Chen Gensi (24 years old, local, residing in a bungalow without a number in the Lu Family Alley of Jaxi Road, French Concession, works as a painter) traveled together at 7:00 PM on the 21st, wearing uniforms. They boarded Tram No. 40 on Route 6 of the French Tram Company outside the Little North Gate of the French Concession, heading to Xieqiao. Chen et al. were on duty and patrolling at the corps headquarters. After boarding the tram, Chen et al. relied on wearing uniforms and refused to purchase tickets. Mu Xiaoshan, the conductor No. 218 (32 years old, Nanjing, residing at No. 6 Defengli, Xietu Road, Huajie), ordered Chen et al. to purchase tickets. Chen et al. refused, and the two sides began to argue. The tram traveled quickly and arrived at Xieqiao Station in the blink of an eye. The two Chens got off the tram angrily and gathered nearly ten colleagues, driving to Xujiahui Road on the border of the Chinese and French Concessions to wait for revenge. At 7:20, Tram No. 40 on Route 6 of the French Tram Company had turned around from the last stop of Luban Road, Lujiawan, Xujiahui Road and was heading to the 16th Pier. When it drove to the station at the intersection of Xujiahui Road and Beile Road, the conductor got off the tram to signal with a red and green light, waiting to hand over the tram. Chen Huaxiang and Chen Genbin had gathered a crowd and rushed over. They boarded the tram without asking any questions and forcibly dragged conductor Mu Xiaoshan No. 218 off the tram, pulling him into the open space leveled on the bank of the Lujiabang River, between Xieshi Road and Xujiahui. Mu was pushed to the ground and beaten with fists and feet by many people. Some people held two pistols to watch out. At that time, Mu was kicked in the abdomen by leather shoes and stabbed in the abdomen and left corner of the head with the bayonet of the gun, suffering serious injuries and falling to the ground. When he was beaten, Mu shouted for help loudly. The patrol No. 87 of the Vietnamese police sent by the nearby French Police Station reported to the French Police Station by telephone. When the police station dispatched a large number of detectives to arrest the suspects, the perpetrators had scattered and fled. Only the victim, conductor Mu Xiaoshan No. 218, was seen lying on the ground seriously injured, with fresh blood gushing from the wounds. He was immediately sent to Guangci Hospital. The French Police Station reported to the French Consulate. It was found that the main culprits were Chen Huaxiang and Chen Gendou. They were detained in Qiaojiabang, Nanshi. The French Police Station notified the French Police Station on the afternoon of the next day. Detectives Zhou Buguang and Zhong Benchang et al. went to transfer the two Chens to their custody. Yesterday noon, they were sent to the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. Fei Xizhen, a lawyer from the Police Department, stated the case, requesting that the defendants be detained, the investigation be rescheduled, the accomplices be arrested, and a lawsuit be filed. He also said that the victim was currently being treated in the hospital and was seriously injured, so he could not be present in court. Subsequently, detectives Zhou Buguang and Zhong Benchang et al. reported the details of the incident and the circumstances of the arrest of the defendants. Judge Wang Gangxu reviewed the report and ordered the defendants to be questioned separately. Both Chens denied the charges, claiming that the assault was committed by comrades who went to seek revenge after hearing about our complaints. The court reviewed the confessions and ordered that the trial be rescheduled for further investigation. The defendants were returned to custody. A forensic doctor will be sent to the hospital with the police detectives to verify the victim's injuries.

Female Gambling Boss Lu Laoqi's Trial Record; Murder Case Dropped Due to Lack of Evidence, Gambling Case Prosecuted Under Criminal Law

Lu Laoqi, alias Wenying, 35 years old, local, the female gambling boss wanted by the police, previously opened a salted meat shop and brothel at No. 114 Aige Road. She was wanted by the Second Special Court at the request of the French Police Station for opening gambling games and inciting the assassination of Shao Wenbin, a fellow gambler. She had evaded arrest for two years. Until 9:00 PM on the 5th of this month, Lu went to No. 5 Yurenli, Yunnan Road, British Concession, where she was discovered by Qian Chenglong, an inspector of the French Police Station, who led detectives Zhang Ziying, Xie Guangming, and Wang Dongwan to arrest her with the assistance of the Old Zha Police Station. She was brought to the Second Special Court, where Judge Zhang Chaozuo held two hearings. The case was reported to the police, and the case was postponed due to the incomplete investigation procedures of the French Police Department. Yesterday morning, the case was heard again. Since the original presiding judge Zhang Chaozuo was transferred to the Civil Division, Wang Gangxu, the chief of the Criminal Division, accompanied by clerk Gao Yanmao, came to the Criminal Division to interrogate her. Lu confessed her name as Wenying, her childhood name as Shicui, so people called her Aqi, 35 years old, from Nanxiang, residing at No. 55 Hu Family Pavilion, Fahua, her husband had died. At this point, Fei Xizhen, a lawyer from the Police Department, stated the case, saying that the defendant's arrest warrant was signed by the court on November 7, 1932, and she was only arrested now. The defendant, together with Gao Lansheng, Mao Axiang, Shi Laohu, Qian Ajin, and other gambling offenders who had been arrested and punished, jointly organized a large gambling house, as evidenced by the confessions of Gu Gengsheng, Hua Amao, and others who had been arrested and punished. Regarding the suspicion of inciting murder, after the Police Department questioned Zhang Bingrong, the murderer in the Shao Wenbin case, there was no active evidence of criminal suspicion, so she was not prosecuted. She is now prosecuted for gambling under Article 268 of the Criminal Law. Lu confessed that when she opened the salted meat shop in March 1933, a guest named Xiao Pengtou came and said that he had opened a gambling den in the city, Chinese territory, and invited me to invest in shares, each share costing ten yuan. I did not agree to pay. Later, money was distributed to me. In mid-May, the police station found out and sent detectives to search my place, but they did not find any evidence. Later, the guest came again and was rejected. From then on, I closed the door (Han Zhuang) and moved elsewhere. The gambling den was not a large one. I met Mao Axiang at the age of nineteen, and his wife was my little sister. I did not know Gao Lansheng. I heard that he was a warehouse worker. At that time, I heard that the large gambling house was Gao Lansheng's. I did not know that Mao Axiang was running gambling games. The official asked if she knew the gambling offenders Gu Gengsheng and Hua Amao. She replied that she did not. The court reviewed the confessions and decided to reschedule the hearing for the 27th because the case still needed investigation. Lu also requested the court, saying that she had sores on her hands and had an old mother and children at home. Could she be allowed to post bail? Lu's lawyers, Jiang Yiping and Ma Shouhua, also made a legal request for Lu to post bail on her behalf. The court ordered the defendant to postpone bail and return to the detention center.

Shao and young woman Chen Aidi recently hired lawyer Zhang Binqiu to file a private prosecution with the Criminal Court of the District Court against her husband Lu Qinshu and father-in-law Lu Yunjie for bigamy and abandonment. Please Return Managed Inheritance: Li Nongjiu Accuses His Biological Father; Mediation Fails at Special Second Court Yesterday; Father's Side Claims Managed Property Is Not as Much

Li Nongjiu, a 37-year-old wealthy man from Anhui residing at No. 66 Yongji Lane, Wangzhi Road, in the French Concession, lives off rental properties. Recently, he, represented by lawyers Jiang Yiping and Hua Maosheng, filed a petition with the Civil Division of the Special Second Court against his father, Li Fengchi (nearly 70 years old, residing at No. 15 Dumei Villa, Dumei Road, a shareholder of Shanghai Xinhua Bank), seeking the return of inheritance. According to the petition, the respondent is the petitioner's biological father. In the seventh year of the Republic of China, the petitioner was adopted by the late Madam Pan as the heir of his late uncle, Zijing Gong. All of Zijing Gong's property was managed by Madam Pan. After Madam Pan passed away last year, the respondent, using the excuse that the property was of great value and could lead to family disputes, took control of the entire property, valued at over 200,000, under the pretext of temporarily managing it. He claimed that once the funeral arrangements were completed, he would hand it over to the petitioner for self-management. The petitioner, out of filial piety, initially did not suspect any ulterior motives. However, the respondent, with ulterior motives, publicly stated that the property should be equally inherited by the petitioner and his half-sister, Zonghui, born to his stepmother, and refused to allow the petitioner to interfere in any way. Recently, he even instigated Zonghui to file a lawsuit with your court for property division, falsely claiming that the inherited property was only 40,000, which your court has already rejected and recorded. The petitioner requests that the respondent be summoned to court for mediation, ordering him to hand over all the property to the petitioner for management. The court, based on the petition, summoned both parties to court yesterday afternoon for mediation in the fourth courtroom, presided over by Judge Zhang Chaozuo. Both parties were represented by lawyers. First, the petitioner's lawyer, Hua Maosheng, stated the petitioner's intention for mediation and presented a list of the property. The respondent's lawyer claimed that the property managed by the respondent was not as much as listed and opposed the mediation and handover. Judge Zhang, after reviewing the statements, concluded that mediation was not possible and declared the mediation unsuccessful, instructing a formal lawsuit to be filed according to the law, and adjourned the court.

Today, Christmas is Celebrated Vigorously in Catholic Churches Throughout the City

Christmas, one of the four major holidays of the Catholic Church, has been celebrated by Catholics around the world since Pope Julius I designated December 25th as the day for celebration in the fourth century. This morning at midnight, more than twenty Catholic churches throughout the city held midnight Mass. Believers flocked to nearby churches in the dark of night to participate in the service, commemorating the shepherds' eager visit upon Jesus' birth at midnight. The churches were decorated with nativity scenes in caves, illuminated by candles, with believers praying, chanting scriptures, and singing hymns, creating a lively atmosphere. Believers also fasted and prepared themselves the day before. As for drunken revelry and fictitious customs such as Santa Claus, they are all rejected by the Catholic Church. Instead, the church advocates charitable acts for children and the poor, in accordance with the Savior's doctrine of universal love. The Catholic Youth Association of Dongjiadu, Nanbu, held a carnival starting at 7:30 last night to celebrate the occasion.

Zhuanqiao Civil Education Center Sends Letters to Farmers on Key Points for Raising and Caring for Draft Cattle

The Zhuanqiao Civil Education Center in Shanghai County sent letters to farmers raising cattle in the district yesterday, stating: "Greetings, the proper raising and care of draft cattle are closely related to our well-being and the health of the cattle. Here are eight key points to pay attention to, please refer to them to improve the health of your cattle and increase their work efficiency." The eight key points are listed below:

"Love" Draft cattle are the farm's laborers and the farmer's assistants. We rely on them to share all the work in the fields, so the abundance of the harvest and the prosperity of the countryside are directly and indirectly related to them. This is a very important matter. Therefore, their health is the farmer's fortune, and their longevity is the farmer's welfare. Farmers should treat them as close friends and not as slaves.

"Feeding" In the spring, summer, and autumn when there is plenty of green grass, we can rely entirely on grazing to save on feed. In winter, when the grass is withered, we can feed them dry grass, such as rice straw and beanstalks. However, when work is busy, we should give them some refined food such as wheat bran and soybean cake, depending on the workload.

"Diet" The feed and drinking water for draft cattle must be clean and fresh. Add appropriate amounts of salt and charcoal at regular intervals. The feeding time should be fixed and unchanged. When changing feed, it should be done gradually and not too hastily.

"Brushing" Draft cattle often have sweat secretions and dirt clinging to their bodies, which not only hinders their bodily functions but also decomposes the dirt, irritating the skin and easily attracting diseases. Therefore, the body surface of draft cattle should be brushed daily to keep them clean and hygienic.

"Hoof Trimming" Draft cattle's hooves should be trimmed regularly and not allowed to grow excessively. If the hoof shape changes and the ability decreases, they should be trimmed regularly to maintain their health. Pay attention to cracks in the hoof surface and the blockage of debris on a daily basis.

"Comfort" Draft cattle cannot have a good life without a comfortable environment. Therefore, the cattle shed must be bright and have adequate sunlight every day. Manure and dirt must be cleaned up at any time to prevent accumulation. In addition, attention must be paid to air circulation and protection from wind and rain.

"Exercise" Draft cattle, especially in the cold winter, should have adequate exercise in open spaces every day. This is the secret to maintaining their health. If they are confined to the cattle shed all day, eating and doing nothing, even if they are well managed and fed well, their muscles will become weak, gradually losing their disease resistance and work efficiency.

"Disease" If draft cattle unfortunately experience abnormal conditions, such as dryness of the nasal mirror, cessation of rumination, vomiting, or diarrhea, a veterinarian should be called immediately for diagnosis and treatment.

Two Robbery Cases in Nanshi: One Thief and Stolen Gun Recovered

A gray overcoat was stolen from the Mingxing Clothing Company on Ximen Fangxie Road. The patrolling police recovered a thief and the stolen gun. Property was stolen from Cai Yuji Woodenware Store on Minguo Road outside Lao Beimen, and the thieves escaped without a trace. The details of the incidents, as learned by a reporter from Guomin News Agency, are as follows:

One Thief Apprehended: Ma Miaogen, a 33-year-old from Pudong, residing at No. 199 Ximen Fangxie Road, owns the Mingxing Clothing Company. Around 8 o'clock yesterday morning, three robbers speaking the local dialect, wearing black long gowns and blue cloth long coats, arrived. One robber guarded the door, while two robbers broke into the store and, pretending to ask about the boss, pulled out guns and threatened the staff, including Wei Aisheng. They forcibly snatched a gray overcoat with blue satin lining, a small red silk cashmere cloak with white leather collar, and other items from the glass display window. Except for one robber who escaped through the back door by taking the night soil bucket, another robber fled out of the main gate. Just as Jin Fu, an apprentice from the upstairs leather box shop, shouted to catch the thief, Wu Kun, a patrolling officer from the Fangxie Road Post No. 10 of the West Fighting Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, heard the alarm and gave chase. In a desperate attempt to escape, the thief, heading north to south, threw away the stolen goods at the entrance of Yihe Lane and fled into the alley. Woodenware Store: At the Cai Yuji Woodenware Store, No. 941 Minguo Road outside Lao Beimen, around 9 o'clock the night before, three robbers wearing blue cloth short shirts and trousers and gray cloth long gowns, also speaking the local dialect, armed with weapons, went to the store to rob. In order to promote the natural gas vehicle industry and prevent fuel leakage in automobiles, the Jiangsu Provincial Highway Administration designated the Sujia Road for pilot use. The test will evaluate the vehicles' load capacity, speed, fuel consumption, and climbing ability to determine their superiority.

Dr. Wang Boqi: All Executive and Supervisory Committee Members of the Rice Merchants Association Advise Fellow Traders to Cancel Broadcasting

The Shanghai Rice Merchants Association has repeatedly received reports from a majority of member traders that several traders have recently used broadcasting methods to promote low prices, which is in conflict with trade regulations. Moreover, the prices are confused and inconsistent, and the advertised prices do not match the true market prices, making it difficult for outsiders to distinguish between truth and falsehood, disrupting market prices, and damaging credibility. The association convened a joint meeting of all executive and supervisory committee members and the directors and deputy directors of each district office the other day. It was decided that all executive and supervisory committee members would personally visit each rice shop that broadcasts to advise them to cancel broadcasting. Yesterday at 1:00 pm, the rice shops that broadcast were advised earnestly, and the reasons were explained in detail. The owners and managers of each rice shop understood the importance of the matter and agreed to cancel radio broadcasting immediately. They wrote voluntary letters of commitment, signed and sealed them, and handed them over to the committee members for preservation, to ensure compliance. In addition to the satisfactory results today, it was decided that if any unscrupulous traders imitate them in the future, the association will submit a request for severe sanctions in accordance with the four items of announcement decree No. 10897 of the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs.

Case of French Concession Detective Insulting a Legitimate Businessman Named Fan: Fellow Townsmen's Association Expresses Indignation; Sends Letter to Authorities Yesterday Demanding Strict Punishment

Fan Tingzhang, a native of Zhenhai, and his cousin Fan Wenzhao, on the 6th of this month, were mediating a dispute between their younger sister Zhang Fan and a tenant Yu Xisheng, residing at No. 8 Youde Lane, Malong Road. French Concession detective Wang Dongming, without asking the reason, arrested the Fan brothers, handcuffed them, and sent them to the Lujiawan Police Station. After questioning and clarifying that they were not involved, they were advised to leave. The Fan brothers are legitimate businessmen and suffered this strange humiliation, which was difficult to bear. They hired lawyer Sun Zukang to file a private prosecution with the First Special District Court against detective Wang Dongming for illegally handcuffing them, obstructing their freedom, and publicly insulting them, and reported the matter to the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Townsmen's Association for assistance. It is reported that the members of the association were indignant upon hearing the complaint. Yesterday, they sent separate letters to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Second Special District Court and the Police Department of the French Concession Board of Works, demanding that the detective be strictly punished according to the law, to prevent illegal activities and protect human rights. The letter stated: "Greetings, according to a letter from our members Fan Tingzhang and Fan Wenzhao, Tingzhang and Wenzhao are legitimate businessmen, operating businesses and serving as managers. Zhang Fan, who resides at No. 8 Youde Lane, Malong Road, is Tingzhang's younger sister and Wenzhao's cousin. In March of this year, tenant Yu Xisheng rented the front building from her. Since moving in, he has been repeatedly investigated and searched by the police due to certain suspicions. On the 1st of this month, he was searched again. Although no contraband was found, Zhang Fan was greatly alarmed and had no choice but to negotiate with Yu Xisheng to move out. Not only did he refuse, but on the 6th of this month, he gathered his mother-in-law, wife, and brother-in-law Xiang Tianbao and others to use force, injuring Zhang Fan's niece, who was sent to the police station for punishment before returning home, making a big scene. Upon hearing the news, Tingzhang and Wenzhao, as relatives, went to mediate and saw Yu Xisheng and the hooligans he had summoned were arguing with Zhang Fan. Tingzhang and Wenzhao, fearing a major disaster, reported to the police and requested assistance. Unexpectedly, on the way, the defendant Wang Dongming suddenly appeared, claiming to be a detective sent by the police station to investigate. Without asking the reason, he disregarded the tenants who were arguing and handcuffed Tingzhang and Wenzhao, displaying great arrogance, as if they were thieves. Tingzhang and Wenzhao were shocked and did not know why they were being blamed. They told him the truth and showed him their name cards to prove their identity, but he not only did not understand but even used his fists and feet. Then, he dragged Tingzhang and Wenzhao to the Lujiawan Police Station. Along the way, they passed through the busy city, and onlookers were numerous. The humiliation suffered by Tingzhang and Wenzhao was unprecedented and caused them great pain. After arriving at the police station, after inquiring and clarifying that they were not involved, they were told to leave. Tingzhang and Wenzhao then questioned the police station, stating that they were the ones who came to the police station to report the incident, and were not present at the argument, nor were they caught in the act. The detective did not investigate and handcuffed and arrested them, which is clearly an abuse of power and a violation of the law. The police officers had no words to answer and only comforted them. It is thought that the freedom of action of the people should not be interfered with without legal grounds and unavoidable circumstances. This is the constitution of a civilized country. Although the Public Concession has special circumstances, the police's exercise of the power of arrest should also be within the scope of the law. Detective Wang Dongming, who serves in the police station, without asking the reason, arbitrarily arrested innocent businessmen, handcuffed and insulted them, deprived them of their freedom, and abused the law for personal gain. If he is not punished immediately, the residents of the concession will be in danger. In addition to filing a private prosecution with the court in accordance with the law, please uphold justice and provide assistance. The circumstances of the letter have been brought to the association. Check that Fan Tingzhang and Wenzhao are both legitimate businessmen, abiding by the law and known to all fellow villagers. Today, they were wantonly trampled on by the detective, and the members of our association are all indignant. In addition to writing to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association, a special letter is sent to your Chief Inspector to investigate the matter thoroughly, first suspending the detective from his duties, and then transferring him to the court according to the law for punishment, to prevent illegal activities and protect human rights. Please enforce public punishment deeply. This is addressed to the Chief Inspector of the Police Department of the French Concession Board of Works. From Yu Hede, committee member of the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Townsmen's Association.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast for 4:30 PM yesterday is as follows: Shandong and surrounding areas are clear and cold, with strong northwest to north winds. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River are overcast and cold, with fog and a risk of snow; wind direction is unstable. The center of the hurricane at 2:00 PM was located within approximately 60 miles of 14 degrees North latitude and 120 degrees East longitude; wind strength is unknown. Furthermore, the highest temperature in Shanghai during the 24 hours prior to 3:00 PM yesterday was 40.5 degrees, and the lowest was 29.7 degrees. The highest and lowest temperatures on the same day last year were 51.6 and 42.8 degrees, respectively. A climate forecast for the week of Christmas: The first half of the period will have unstable and cold weather, with light and directionless winds and light fog, with a risk of snow. The second half of the period will change from overcast to cloudy, becoming colder, with increasing fog and variable winds from northwest to northeast.

An Overview of the Shanghai Flour Industry (No. 7 in the Overview of Shanghai Industry and Commerce)

— Edited by the China Credit Information Service

1. The Rise and Fall of the Shanghai Flour Industry

In the past, traditional Chinese flour production relied on stone mills. In rural areas, farmers would often prepare their own mills and make flour themselves, while in towns there were so-called grinding shops. These grinding shops were a combination of shops and manual workshops, usually equipped with one, two, or three mills powered by livestock. In addition, in rural areas, there were also water mills that used the power of streams to turn the stone mills, which were widely used by farmers. However, all these traditional methods were far inferior to modern mechanical milling in terms of speed and the quality of the flour produced. Therefore, since the introduction of foreign flour and modern milling techniques into China, their position has gradually declined. Although water mills still exist today, they are no longer as important as they once were.

Shanghai, being the commercial hub of the country, was the first to see the import of foreign flour and the emergence of modern factories. The initial import of foreign flour by foreign merchants was to supplement food supplies, and they requested the Qing government to exempt import duties. In the 22nd year of the Guangxu Emperor's reign (1896), a German merchant came to Shanghai and established the Zengyu Flour Company (which closed down in 1926). They directly manufactured flour in China, using small carts to deliver the flour and encourage people to try it, marking the beginning of the modern flour manufacturing industry in China. In the 24th year of Guangxu's reign (1898), Chinese merchants followed suit and established the Fufeng Machinery Flour Company in Shanghai. Subsequently, many Chinese merchants joined the industry. The following table lists the companies established in Shanghai over the years:

Period of Establishment　Number of Establishments　Notes

Guangxu 22nd to 27th Year　Two　——

Guangxu 28th to 32nd Year　Four　——

Guangxu 33rd Year to Xuantong 3rd Year　Two　One was reorganized

Years 1 to 5 of the Republic of China　Nine

Years 6 to 10 of the Republic of China　Six　——

Years 10 to 15 of the Republic of China　Four　Three were reorganized

Years 16 to 20 of the Republic of China　One　——

Years 21 to 24 of the Republic of China　Zero　——

Note: This table is adapted from the Jiangsu Business Records.

From the table above, we can see that the most prosperous period for Shanghai's emerging national flour industry was between the 1st and 10th years of the Republic of China (1912-1921). Excluding the reorganized ones, there were as many as fourteen completely new establishments. The main reason for this was the outbreak of the European War in 1914, which lasted for five years. During this period, due to the inconvenience of maritime transport and the vast military needs of European and American countries, even self-sufficiency in food supplies was insufficient, let alone exports. As a result, China's flour industry rose rapidly, creating its golden age. However, after the end of the war, the objective situation changed immediately. Few new factories emerged; in fact, only two completely new establishments were founded between 1922 and 1931. At the same time, the signs of decline also began to appear. For example, Yufeng, established in the 30th year of Guangxu's reign (1904), Dayou, established in the 1st year of the Republic of China (1912), Xinchang, established in the 3rd year of the Republic of China (1914), Changfeng, established in the 5th year of the Republic of China (1916), and Yuanfeng, established in the 7th year of the Republic of China (1918), all declared bankruptcy around 1926. In 1931, after the "September 18th Incident," the following year saw the Battle of Shanghai. Simultaneously, domestic and international economic panics struck one after another, making the situation for Shanghai's flour industry even more unbearable. It is recalled that when the Battle of Shanghai broke out, the Wusong Flour Mill, established less than a year before, had all its factory buildings and machinery destroyed by fire, resulting in losses of over 200,000 yuan. Although the Zhonghua Fengji Flour Mill, located in Tanziwan, was spared, stray bullets still caused losses of tens of thousands. Other factories, such as Shenda in Nanshi, Fuxin north of the New Bridge, Yutong on Guangfu Road, and Xiangxin Lida in Caojiadu and Xiaoshadu, were either occupied by soldiers or used to store munitions. Although they did not suffer the devastation of gunfire, the losses they sustained were significant. As for the losses caused by the stagnation of business due to military reasons, they are difficult to calculate. In recent years, the economic panic has not yet been restored, the purchasing power of the people is weak, and the burden of taxes and levies is heavy. It is common to hear of Shanghai flour mills declaring closure or suspension of work. For example, Xiangxin Changji and Haifeng Xinji declared liquidation in May and June of last year, while Huafeng Xingji and Zhonghua Longji suspended work in March and October of this year. This month alone, Xinda and Xinji flour companies have also simultaneously announced their closure. Therefore, the future of the flour industry does not seem optimistic.

2. The Actual Situation of Shanghai Flour Mills

As previously stated, Shanghai's flour industry is the largest in the country. According to the Shanghai Yearbook of 1935, its actual position is as shown in the following table:

Number of Mills　Capital　Annual Flour Production

Shanghai　12　6,089,000 Yuan　29,720,000 Bags

National　66　14,552,000 Yuan　64,963,000 Bags

From the table above, we can observe that more than one-fifth of the country's machine-made flour mills are located in Shanghai, with Shanghai accounting for more than one-quarter of the total capital. Shanghai's annual flour production accounts for about two-fifths of the national total. This not only proves the importance of Shanghai's flour mills but also indicates the progress of production technology and the scale of production in Shanghai, as its number of mills accounts for only one-fifth of the total, while its output accounts for two-fifths.

Among the existing mills in Shanghai, the oldest is Fufeng, and the largest in scale are Fuxin and Maoxin. The organizational structure and production and sales of each are described below:

1. Fufeng Machinery Flour Company: Located at Chedaijiao in the city, it was established in the 24th year of Guangxu's reign (1898). It is a limited liability company with a capital of one million yuan. The general manager is Mr. Sun Jun. The factory's machinery is comprised of 26 units made in America and 560 units made in England. On average, it can produce about 8.5 million bags of flour and 960,000 bags of bran per year. The brands include Blue and Red Bicycle (also known as Old Car Plate), Green Fort, Phoenix Playing with Peony, Green Double Fish, and Green Double Tiger. The Old Car Plate brand is the most expensive and sells well in Tianjin, Guangdong, and other areas. The bran is sold throughout the interior. The profits for the last three years are as follows: 258,267 yuan in 1932, 258,442 yuan in 1933, and 305,173 yuan in 1934, and the trend is continuing to increase. The Yutong Fufeng Company on Guangfu Road in Zhabei is also operated by the factory. It was leased from the late wealthy businessman Zhu Youhong on the Dragon Boat Festival in 1926. Yutong now has a capital of 500,000 yuan, with Sun Zhongli as the manager and Xue Qinzhou as the factory director. The machinery in the factory is made in America, with a total of 24 units. On average, it produces 164,000 bags of flour and 180,000 bags of bran per year. The brand name is the same as Fufeng's Old Car Plate, and the sales market is mainly Tianjin, followed by Shanghai. In addition, the Shanghai Pudong Warehouse is also operated by Fufeng Company. (To be continued)
