The Impact of the 1935-36 Basketball Rules on Basketball Training (Part 1)

— Written by Ruby of the United States, Translated by Qian Yiqin

What impact will the new basketball rules have on coaches? Will currently effective offensive methods lose their effectiveness due to the changes in the rules? What kind of offensive and defensive strategies will succeed? All these questions are answered by Mr. J. Craig Ruby, the long-time head coach of the University of Illinois—Translator.

At the meeting of the National Basketball Coaches Association held in May of this year, Mr. Nat Holman of the City College of New York reported that the greatest difficulty for referees in the eastern states of the United States was the constant struggle for position between the pivot player and the opposing defender when the ball had not yet been passed to the pivot position. Sometimes, this struggle for position resembled a wrestling match. The Association passed Mr. Holman's proposal—that the three-second rule for the pivot player on the offensive side, whether he is holding the ball or not, should be effective—and recommended it to the National Basketball Committee (Note: This Committee is the highest organization that amends the basketball rules every year. The rules in our country are based on this). The Committee has incorporated this proposal into the 1935-36 rules.

The main point of this new rule is that "when a player on a team is controlling or has obtained the ball during the game, a player, whether he is holding the ball or not, must not remain in the free throw area for more than three seconds. When a player on one team passes the ball to another player, the ball is considered to be under the control of that team" (Note 1). This, of course, refers to when a player on the offensive side enters his free throw area, the three-second count immediately begins. If he receives the ball and dribbles it, he must also run out of the area within a one-second limit, otherwise his team will lose possession of the ball and be called out of bounds. If he shoots immediately after receiving the ball, the three-second count ends, because his team no longer controls the ball. When the ball bounces off the backboard, anyone can remain in that area at will.

This rule has a huge impact on the game. From now on, we will no longer see burly players standing in the free throw area, relying on their height and reach, and competing with defenders for unobstructed opportunities to receive the ball. In the future, if you still want to use a simple pivot offense, the player playing pivot must have good footwork and proper timing in order to receive the ball unimpeded. Figure 1 shows a style of action that is suitable for a pivot player. When No. 4 dribbles forward, pivot player No. 1 runs straight forward over the area, then turns back, pretending to run back, and then turns to the left and moves forward, calculating the time to receive the pass from No. 2. In the first place, number 2 has already received the ball passed by number 4. After No. 1 passes the ball to No. 2 (or No. 4), he must quickly run out of the free throw area, otherwise the three-second rule will cause his team to lose possession of the ball. If No. 2 receives the ball as shown in the figure, he must also run out of the area within three seconds.

Many coaches have asked about player No. 1, if he puts one foot outside the free throw line while the other foot is inside the area, and raises the foot inside the area every one or two seconds to avoid the three-second rule, is that legal? Or they ask if player No. 1 runs with one foot outside the line and one foot inside the free throw circle, is all the time considered to be within the three-second count? The explanation of the rule is as follows: "When team A gets the ball, one foot of A1 is inside the area, and as he rotates, he completely moves outside the area, and finally turns back into the area. According to the rules, if this entire action takes more than three seconds, it is a violation" (Note 2). Therefore, in the above situation, it is not legal.

Because the three-second rule is sufficient to affect the offensive methods of the pivot player, the defender guarding him must also change his strategy. Or the guard defending No. 1 in Figure 1 will adopt a position that hinders No. 1's movement. This will inevitably force player No. 1 to develop true footwork and proper timing. Or this new rule will only move the struggle for position between No. 1 and its guard from inside the free throw area to the outside of the area. If that is true, then this rule will hardly achieve its original purpose.

Assuming that this simple pivot offense can still be used freely under the implementation of this new rule, at least two currently well-known offenses

Figure 1

methods will be eliminated. Figure 2 shows a famous forward's exchange offense in front of the pivot player. No. 4 passes the ball to No. 1. When No. 3 passes in front of No. 1, No. 1 pretends to pass the ball to him, but in fact passes it to No. 2, who passes in front of him a second time. From repeated tests, from No. 1 entering the area until he passes it to No. 2 and he himself runs out of the area, or until No. 2 shoots, it takes more than three seconds.

Figure 2

Educational News

Recent News from the National Institute for Compilation and Translation Regarding Translated Terminology

The recent progress of the National Institute for Compilation and Translation in its terminology translation work is as follows: Since Mr. Zuo Renxia, along with Mr. Zhao Yan, began compiling psychological terminology, progress has been very rapid. The complete standard psychological terminology has now been completed, totaling approximately three thousand terms, and has been printed. It will soon be distributed to domestic psychology experts to solicit opinions. The compilation of terminology for psychological instruments and equipment is now planned to begin, with an estimated three thousand terms. The first draft is expected to be completed in three months. The first ten parts of chemical engineering terminology have been distributed to relevant institutions and organizations to solicit opinions. Furthermore, the Chinese Institute of Chemical Engineers, the Chinese Chemical Society, and the Chinese Chemical Industry Association have each been requested to nominate six representatives to form a joint committee for chemical engineering terminology. The first draft has already been reviewed by experts, and over twenty copies have been returned. Recently, more than ten additional review copies have been returned. For electrical engineering terminology, Chairman Yun Yintang of the terminology review committee has been specially requested to send letters, stipulating that the ordinary and power sections of the terminology be reviewed by the end of January of next year, and that the telecommunications and electrochemistry sections be reviewed by the end of February. For mathematics terminology, printing will commence soon after the presentation of the partial publication. However, since the original manuscript was compiled based on academic disciplines, checking was quite inconvenient. Therefore, the Chinese Mathematical Society was consulted, and it was agreed that all terminology would be re-arranged alphabetically for ease of reference. This re-arrangement procedure is quite cumbersome, but is largely complete. After one more round of sorting and proofreading, it can be officially printed. The first draft of human anatomy terminology comprises 522 pages, with approximately six thousand terms. It has been distributed to the review committee members for review. Regarding botanical terminology, a total of 12,270 cards have been received from Mr. Wang Zengjia, sent from Peiping. They are currently being organized. The reviewed draft of geological terminology has been printed and distributed to committee members for a second review. For mineralogical terminology, both the first and revised proofs have been checked since typesetting began. The compilation of Chinese-Western indexes is currently being rushed.

Shandong Province's Rural Education Experiment

In order to effectively promote rural education in Shandong Province, the Shandong Provincial Rural Education Guidance Committee was organized last year to carry out a planned initiative. As a result, thirty counties in the province were designated as rural education experimental zones. In April of this year, the Shandong County Administration Construction Experimental Zone Administrative Commissioner's Office was established, designating fourteen counties in western Shandong as experimental zones for construction. To unify authority, the rural education experimental zones of Jining, Chengwu, Shanxian, Cao County, and others were transferred to the jurisdiction of the twenty-six counties, including Licheng. The experimental zone funding for each county comes from a portion of the county education funds and the county public education center operating expenses, as well as the funds of elementary schools within the central primary school district. The funding for the Linyi and Ziyang experimental zones is formed by the complete merger of the old experimental zone funding and the funding of the affiliated elementary school of the normal school. The funding for these two county zones is over ten thousand yuan. For the other experimental zones, the highest annual funding is 7,810 yuan (Zhangqiu) and the lowest is 1,626 yuan (Zou County). The work of the experimental zones begins with language education. Because the tradition of respecting teachers and valuing education still exists in rural areas, if schools can be managed effectively, it will promote farmers' faith and facilitate progress. Therefore, the initial work involves focusing on improving the central primary school where the office is located and promoting the central primary school's experience to other primary schools within the district and in rural society using effective methods. In terms of teaching, school education includes central primary schools, rural primary schools, short-term primary schools, public classes, and women's classes. Social education includes open-air schools, little teacher instruction, reading rooms, public libraries, lecture halls, wall newspapers, letter-writing and learning assistance centers, and mobile libraries. Secondly, recreational education is implemented, such as providing medical care through mobile medicine chests and establishing martial arts societies, which are very well-received by farmers. Next is livelihood education, which involves establishing small-scale farms, livestock farms, contracted farmland (experimental crops are mainly wheat and cotton), experimenting with the eradication of diseases and pests, establishing vocational training classes, promoting family side occupations, and cooperative enterprises. The best work of the rural education experimental zones in the past year in various counties of the province, in addition to running school education, has been to gradually set up rural undertakings and engage in the development of rural industries. There are five key steps for the future development of agricultural production in the twenty-fourth year: Investigate the types and quantities of various foreign goods imported into each experimental zone. Investigate the local specialties and products that can replace foreign goods within the zone, along with their quantities and sales methods. Conduct a detailed statistical analysis based on the investigation. Organize production and marketing cooperatives separately. Gather the investigative statistics from each experimental zone and contact banks for investment, in order to secure loans for the development of industries. The current work of each experimental zone is focused on diligently investigating and gathering statistics, while the future work will actively focus on cooperative organization and contacting the banking industry for investment.

Children's Education Novel

Little Men (1)(3)(4)

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Nan then quickly turned around, re-tied himself, and began sewing energetically. Soon, Rob came along, and finding the new punishment amusing, he took a jump rope and tied himself to the other leg of the sofa. It was rare to see him so amiable and considerate.

"I got lost too, so I should be punished like Nan," he explained to his mother when she discovered the new offender.

"I'm afraid you do deserve some punishment, because you knew it wasn't right to run so far away from the others."

"Nan went with me," Rob said, though willing to taste the new penalty, he was unwilling to share the blame.

"You didn't have to go. You have your own sense, even though you're still a little boy. You must always pay attention and listen to the command of your sense or conscience. So you must stay here until lunchtime, and discuss it with Nan. I trust that neither of you will untie yourselves without my permission."

"No, we won't," both said, feeling that it was a virtue to help Mrs. Jo punish themselves.

Shanghai Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School has a long history, and its alumni are located throughout the country and abroad. The alumni residing in Beijing are particularly numerous. Furthermore, the school's basketball team had originally planned to travel to Beiping the day before yesterday, but after receiving a letter from the Beiping alumni, the trip has been postponed due to the current situation.

Financial Clearing Significantly Less Than in Previous Years

The financial sector's year-end closing period is usually much busier than usual. This year is different. Most of the outstanding loans and debts have been settled due to market conditions. Those that remain outstanding are only a small number. All types of collateral loans have a limited term, and the amount due within the year is also limited, no more than three to four million. Other daily transactions will generally be settled by the Lunar New Year's Eve. Therefore, the clearing process has been relatively simple recently. The banks' various procedures are cleared either by the end of the year or by the Lunar New Year's Eve, depending on their circumstances. Therefore, although it is the end of the year, the market atmosphere is not tight. The market activity yesterday was also the same. Interbank lending rates remained at one-tenth (一角) in the morning and afternoon. Interbank draft transactions amounted to over 3.8 million in the morning and over 300,000 in new transactions. Afternoon transactions were over 100,000, and Small General Assembly (小總會) transactions were over 900,000. Banknote issuance was over 1.6 million and over 800,000 to other locations. Foreign collateral loan transactions took back over 900,000 and made over 1.7 million in new loans. Bank receipts: foreign banks received over 2.8 million in draft funds, over 3.3 million in various goods, foreign exchange, and miscellaneous funds, over 800,000 in telegraphic transfers, and over 900,000 in special exchange funds. Chinese banks received over 2.7 million in draft funds, over 3.1 million in various goods, foreign exchange, tax, and miscellaneous funds, over 900,000 in telegraphic transfers, and over 800,000 in special exchange funds. Yarn Trading Holiday Today

Four Days of Annual Leave from the 31st

The Shanghai Yarn and Cloth Exchange, as the Lunar New Year approaches, the standard yarn and cotton market will be closed from December 31, 1935, to January 3, 1936, according to regulations. Business will resume as usual on January 4th. Daily receipts and payments for all brokers within the year will use 30-day commercial bills from December 26th. Also today (the 25th) is the Yunnan Uprising Memorial Day, and the yarn and cotton market will be closed for one day.

U.S. Cotton Merchants Supplement Near Months and Sell Distant Months

Yesterday, U.S. cotton opened with gains of 2 to 7 points for all months. Market conditions were stagnant. Most activity involved shifting from near months to distant months. The December contract was quite strong. No delivery notices have been issued yet. Brokers and short positions were supplementing near months and selling October. There was not much arbitraging. Brokers had uncertain intentions. There were few new non-industry accounts. Generally speaking, it seemed that the market was waiting for developments in Washington. Finally, long positions closed out, and the market retraced. As a result, spot prices were unchanged, near months rose 1 to 7 points, and distant months fell 2 to 9 points. British cotton spot prices rose 3 points, and futures prices rose 3 to 4 points. The amounts sold by Indian cotton arbitrageurs and European exporters were absorbed by short covering. Raw cotton prices fell by 0.25 to 0.75 rupees, Omra rose by 0.75 rupees, and White Rose Creek rose by 1 rupee. The original telegram is left. (Telegraph dated 23rd)

Also, according to a Bombay telegram, the opening forecast for White Rose Creek cotton on the 24th was 228 rupees, down half a rupee from the previous day's close.

A Bombay telegram dated the 23rd stated that the number of cotton bales exported from Rangoon last week was 125, all destined for Melbourne.

Grains: Flour and Wheat Long Positions Seek to Exit

In the morning opening of the flour market, prices for all months initially appeared stable and then flat. Chicago wheat quotations were nearly 0.4 yuan, up 0.08 to 0.2 yuan, and Canadian prices were nearly 0.08 to 0.1 yuan. Therefore, at the initial opening, buyers were still active, with near and distant months up about 0.01 yuan. Later, as the closing approached, most customers with long positions closed out their positions, causing the market to weaken again. When the afternoon opening came, prices for all months actually declined step by step. This was because the end of the year was approaching, the situation was unstable, and market sentiment was weak. Many long positions unloaded their positions, causing prices to fall step by step, down 0.04 to 0.05 yuan from the previous day. Going forward, there shouldn't be a special change. December 25th is the Yunnan Restoration Republic Memorial Day, and the market will be closed for one day.

The wheat market was uniformly sluggish for all months. In the morning sessions, buying parties across all months were unloading because the closing was approaching, causing selling prices to fall 0.03 to 0.05 yuan from the previous day. When the afternoon session opened, trading had cleared, and transactions were slow. However, because of the turbulent situation, market affairs were mostly pessimistic, so trading was scarce, and prices also fell sharply. For example, prices for February and March actually fell about 0.1 yuan. Going forward, if the situation clears up, the market can safely pass the end of the year. Current wheat not opening at Guangzhou.

As the end of the year approaches, merchants return to their hometowns, and factories reduce work, all showing signs of winding down. The release of various metal products has also decreased significantly compared to before, so in recent days, the total trading volume in the city has decreased from 4,000 to 5,000 dan (擔) to 2,000 to 3,000 dan, and recently, market trading has only been 1,300 to 1,400 dan. The prices of various goods are declining due to industry colleagues eagerly trying to unload positions. The most severe declines were in bamboo-joint steel bars, British steel plates, East white iron, and new lead wire. Other products, such as I-beams, angle iron, and shear iron, are also struggling to maintain their prices.

The market outlook feels secure.

Casual Notes

Drippings

(Ji Yijie 紀一介)

A Big Pile of Filth

The dates set for the mandated sanitation campaign by the department are May 15th and December 15th. On these days, local party and government agencies, together with the public, conduct a massive cleanup. Door-to-door sanitation inspections are also carried out, and schools even have sanitation propaganda teams. It would be appropriate for all filth to be swept away, and for every household to have a new atmosphere. Who knew that facts would be more convincing than words, and that things would be so completely different? Here, I can't help but think of a few words that the late Central Committee Member Mr. Wu Zhihui said in a speech at the Jiangsu Provincial Medical Administration College last year on "The Urgency of Public Health Construction." The old gentleman described, "A broken mat stuck in the corner of the door, serving as a breeding ground for bedbugs, a broken toilet bowl lid placed under the bed for display, the rope used to tie up ham still hanging high after the ham is eaten, for spiders to spin webs, and the space under the table and beside the bench, all turned into a display of broken shoes. If we inspect each household, we will surely discover a big pile of filth." These words, spoken frankly, are like a descriptive scene of a typical household. I excerpt them here to urge special attention from those conducting sanitation inspections.

Winter Landscape

— Zhou Xian 周賢

The winter sun always faintly shines with a seemingly drowsy light. The withered black tree trunks face the howling seasonal winds, emitting the struggling sounds of strong resistance. One leaf, two leaves, the remaining leaves clinging to the tree, leisurely follow the wind, detaching from the tree and heading southeast. Turning in the wind, turning on the ground, they unfortunately fall into the same fate as the unfortunate group prostrate on the ground, subject to the ruthless trampling of humans, animals, and even insects. Unfortunate indeed, some even fall into mountain valleys, streams, or other inconceivable places, finding a sad and lonely ending forever forgotten by people.

In winter, rain visits the human world more frequently and abundantly than sunlight. The winter rain always falls like threads. All day, it is like being enveloped in the night. In the countryside, there is no crowing of roosters, no barking of dogs, no shouting of children, and no laughter of adults. All there is is a deathly silence. The mountains in the rain, the trees in the rain, the stone bridges, and the houses all stand quietly, standing in the deathly silent air. Sometimes, a small bird lost in the rain, breaking through the silence with its chirping, but it is very brief. The deathly silence conquers everything in the universe again.

In the city, there is no summer, but there is also no winter. The 1936-style cars always slide wildly on the smooth asphalt roads, in the intoxicating neon lights. The girls have forgotten the season, with their chests and legs bare inside and outside their clothes. Indeed, a spring-like smile always floats on the girls' faces. A "winter" character is faintly embellished on the sale flags and sale slogans. However, the majesty of winter can never defeat the electric heaters and radiators in the ivory tower.

Hmm, winter, although it can never invade the ivory tower, but outside of paradise, there are plenty of hells in this human world. Inside the grand hotel is a scene of spring, but separated by a layer of glass, it is filled with the miserable cries of cold and hunger. No, there are also disaster victims with half their bodies floating in the flood, their lives like one leaf, two leaves, the remaining leaves clinging to the tree.

Everything falls into a deathly atmosphere, except for the ivory tower in the city. - In this way, a powerful winter scene is displayed.

The Toilet

— Feng Moni 馮摩尼

A person certainly cannot live without eating, because without food, one cannot live, but; after eating, one must defecate. If one only eats and does not defecate, it will affect the body, and one cannot live. So, no matter who it is, one must eat, and one cannot avoid the trouble of defecating.

Why Bother to Trap Oneself

Because one must defecate after eating, the toilet is naturally indispensable; however, many people in society panic only about the problem of eating, and no one is anxious about defecating, perhaps because one can only defecate after eating.

It is said that: In the past, men or women defecated entirely in the public latrines in the neighborhood; however, it was somewhat awkward for women to go to the latrines. Later, someone finally came up with a toilet like a round stool, which was both elegant and comfortable, and one didn't have to run around; however, this toilet was intended for women, but when men saw this toilet, they were also unwilling to go to the latrines to defecate, because squatting on the latrine was very tiring. So, they also used the toilet. Until now, except for cases of sudden internal urgency that required a trip to the latrine, everyone else uses the toilet.

However, some people, once they sit on the toilet, are unwilling to stand up. They even sit for an extra moment. Sitting and reading the newspaper, puffing on a cigarette, is indeed a unique experience. Some people sit for several hours, feeling more and more interesting the longer they sit. Exactly what it tastes like, only friends who like to sit on the toilet know.

A person is never satisfied. Even with this extremely comfortable toilet, they are still not satisfied, so they want to use a flushing toilet. After defecating, there is no odor, and the filthy fecal liquid is not visible. However, flushing toilets are almost aristocratic. Only the wealthy can enjoy them; others still use this more common toilet.

I still remember when I was studying in a private school as a child, if I couldn't recite the book, the teacher's face, like that of an angry king, was really scary, so I would use the excuse of defecating to sit on the toilet and secretly look at the book, so as not to be reprimanded by the teacher.

The toilet room, filled with foul odor, can provide convenience to many students. I can't help but sigh, the function of the toilet is truly great.

Reading the Classic of Mountains and Seas

— Shu Fan 叔範

Flipping through the Bashe (巴蛇) illustration, the language is extremely absurd, with similar events. Because of concern for home and country, I don't know where the tears come from! I write a long poem, briefly imitating Tao Yuanming (陶泉明), but my emotions and grievances are different. The sea pavilion glares at everything in solitude, and the illustrations of the primordial wilderness are explained with clear eyes; the strange grief chokes the tongue as the snake swallows the elephant, and the story of magpies yielding nests is heartbreaking! The six realms never concerned themselves with tribulations, and the heavens never talked about kindness and revenge: there is a unique absurd pain in the human world, with no place to arrange the heads of brave men.

Little Western Paradise

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 22: Heroic Words Move Rosy Lips, Group of Sisters Gather to Discuss; False Affection Startles Jade Wrist, Bitter Woman Escapes Captivity

Looking from afar in Beihai, I could already see the change in Jia Duocai's face. I didn't understand the reason, but it seemed to relieve a great deal of suppressed anger, and I couldn't help but feel greatly relieved. After these madams entered the room, they began to make noises and argue. Finally, someone called out, "Let's not make a mess. Let Madam Liu and Mr. Jia speak first. If Madam Liu's words need supplementing, we can add a few words." Then, Madam Liu said, "Mr. Jia, I'll get straight to the point. We, these comrades, believe that spending one hundred and fifty yuan to buy a woman as a slave is not something that modern society can tolerate." Jia Duocai said, "How come you all still don't understand? I'm marrying her as a concubine, not buying her as a slave." Madam Liu said, "You're marrying her as a concubine? Where did you get married? Do you have a wife at home?" Jia Duocai said, "It's marrying her as a side wife. What wedding is needed?" Madam Liu said, "What is a side wife? We don't understand." Jia Duocai said, "Let me put it plainly, it's marrying her as a concubine. You think this is my fault. But there are too many people who marry concubines. Is it against the law for me, Jia, to marry a concubine?" Before he could finish the sentence "just a concubine," there was a sudden clatter of tables, chairs, teacups, and teapots. At the same time, the madams started shouting. Jia Duocai was so scared that he ran straight out, shouting, "You can hit and scold as you please, but if you break anything, I'm not afraid you won't pay for it!" With those words, he had already run out of the room, across the hall, and was standing in the corridor. Several of the madams had already followed him out and surrounded him. Jia Duocai looked at everyone and said, "Are you not being reasonable? I yielded to you in the room, which already shows my retreat. Why are you chasing me outside?" Madam Liu waved her hand and said, "Just come in. If the discussion isn't clear, there's still room for negotiation. Can you just run away?" (383)

Short Stories

The Gifts Santa Claus Brings to Children

— Ya Fei

Every year on December 25th, Santa Claus always brings gifts to children as usual. However, this year is a little different. He knows that this year is Children's Year, and the gift should not only be grander but also not be like in previous years, just using some shallow gifts of food and toys to fool the children. At least he has to choose something meaningful to give them.

He got up early this morning and saw that the weather was still clear, but the northwest wind was blowing really hard. So he put on that big red hood, tightened that half-new, half-old red woolen coat, carried a red cloth bundle, and strode out of his house, heading towards the world market.

"What kind of gifts should I buy to give them that would be suitable? Not food or toys, then I have to choose something practical and adaptable to the times..." He is a kind old man, so he is always thinking about the many lovely children in the world. He wants to make every child happy, and he often feels sorry for some poor children who are not happy, but he has no way to make them all equally happy!

The old man walked and thought all the way, but he couldn't think of what gifts he should buy that would benefit the children and that every child would need. He walked into the largest department store in the world market - the World Department Store - opened his eyes to look, and felt that the situation was a bit miserable - the first thing that caught his eye was some weapons for destroying the world and killing humans - guns, cannons, airplanes, warships, bombs, tanks, and many new scientific and chemical inventions that he had never seen before. In short, he couldn't name what these things were. However, he recognized the various masks hanging at the counter, but they were marked as being for adults, not toys for children to wear.

He looked everywhere and saw that none of these things were suitable as gifts for children today. So he went to the last counter to look. This place was very deserted. There were only a few clerks who seemed to be suffering from decadence lying on the counter, and there were no customers. Several kinds of goods were displayed, such as education, personality, effort, struggle, knowledge, courage, honesty, common sense, hygiene, sports, etc., but they were covered with dust, as if they hadn't been cleaned for a long time. He walked over to take a look and felt that these were the gifts he wanted to give to the children in his heart. He picked one up, blew off the dust, and looked at it carefully. But the two clerks were still cold, as if they were laughing at him for buying these things as gifts today as outdated. However, he finally bought each item, and even bought a big package.

Santa Claus carried a big package of gifts, happily walked out of the door of the World Department Store, and walked on the way home against the fierce northwest wind, preparing to distribute them one by one to those lovely children...

He walked on the road, and he seemed to see the smiling faces of a group of little angels!

Notes on What Was Seen

— (Yangzi Jiang)

Once, I passed by Jing'an Temple and saw two beggars begging for money from a Western gentleman on the sidewalk. The two beggars were a boy and a girl, both about fourteen or fifteen years old. They kept shouting:

"Master, Master, please do a good deed!"

Beggars exist in both Eastern and Western countries, so it is not surprising. However, it is really unnecessary to call a Westerner "Master." According to the recent Shanghai Old Shanghai Exhibition, in the late Qing Dynasty, foreigners had to call Chinese officials "Master" and refer to themselves as "barbarians." The current situation is exactly the opposite. Colonial slaves are always wild, so "barbarians" are actually ourselves. Those who used to call themselves "barbarians" are now respectfully called "Western Masters" by the moonlight.

Hearing the beggar children calling the Westerner "Master," I couldn't help but feel a sense of sorrow.

Shenbao Local Supplement

Discussions

Christmas Demands Italy and Abyssinia to Ceasefire

— Fang Yin

According to Havas Rome, 19th: "The Holy See intends to follow the example of the Bolivian-Paraguayan War in South America and demand that Italy and Abyssinia cease fighting on Christmas Day. However, it is doubtful whether this can be done. Regarding this matter, the Holy See has repeatedly consulted with the Italian government. However, due to the recent development of the situation on the African front, there is no possibility of a cessation of hostilities. It is feared that a large-scale battle will occur in the near future."

It is said that religions are mostly kind-hearted, so they oppose and obstruct all inhumane killings, abuses, or cruel acts of war. Therefore, not long ago, I heard of a so-called "World Peace Prayer Meeting" on the market. However, when I see the actions of religious figures, I am actually quite skeptical. After all, there has been the "Crusade" to the east in history, and recently there has been the expedition against Abyssinia starting from the holy city of Rome. Moreover, what can their so-called prayers for peace contribute to the reality today, when imperialists are drawing their swords and flexing their bows?…

This decision by the Roman Catholic Church to demand a ceasefire between Italy and Abyssinia is neither for the sake of maintaining peace nor does it explain that they are supporting the humanitarianism of religious figures. It is simply to embellish the birth of Jesus, hoping that Christmas will not be spent in the midst of bloody fighting and gunpowder. This can truly be said to be the most sincere face of religious figures: Jesus is loving (?), so there should indeed be no unseemly killing wars on Jesus' birthday. Moreover, can we cite the example of the Bolivian-Paraguayan War and the war between the Han-Zhi sects as examples of fulfilling such requests? Regardless of whether the Italian and Abyssinian authorities agree to the request or not, it is still unobjectionable for the Holy See to enjoy this sacred right.

Donations

— Yao Ying

I was calculating the payments for the upcoming solar New Year when Xiaoling rushed to my bedside, pulled open my mosquito net, grabbed the corner of the quilt with her right hand, and yanked it forcefully. Before I could ask a question, she had already opened her mouth:

"Dad! Dad! School will be dismissed tomorrow, and Pastor Lin told us to donate, any amount of money will do. It has to be given to the principal today, Dad! It's to buy toys for the poor children and let them see a movie. The teacher also said that whoever donates the most will be the first place, Dad! Can you donate two foreign coins? Dad! Dad!" I couldn't figure it out for a moment; it hadn't been many days since I donated one yuan for the flood relief, what were we donating for again?

"Well, well, well, Pastor Lin came to give a speech, teaching us to ask our dads to donate, donate to those little children who are suffering, who have no clothes to wear and nothing to eat, donate copper coins for them to buy toys, and also invite them to see a movie. Dad! Pastor Lin is an old man with a beard, he treats us very well, he brought a lot of candy yesterday, one bag for each person. He also calls us little friends, it's so funny." Xiaoling grinned, the kind of innocence revealed made me not have the courage to refuse him.

"Xiaoling, okay, okay, I'll give it to you tomorrow." I planned to think of another way, so as not to make him feel unhappy.

"Dad! It has to be today, tomorrow is dismissal." She said to Mom, "Mom! Dad! He won't give me the foreign coins." "Just give it to him! I've been sewing until dusk last night, I don't have a single penny."

"Go to the wallet and take a look." I spat out these words as if something was stuck in my throat. She lazily walked to the table, picked up the wallet, unbuttoned it, and poured out one silver coin and two jiaos onto the table. Xiaoling ran over and took them in her hand, and said to me again, "Dad, I need one more."

"Xiaoling, just take one, at school, they keep asking for donations, you can't keep donating without end." After being scolded by her mother, Xiaoling walked away in disappointment. I knew that the child was not satisfied, but how could I satisfy his desires? My gaze was seized by the calendar on the wall, the end of the year was already approaching!

Page 16

Dog

— Yan

If a passerby asks for directions to the Zhu Country Gentleman's house, after telling them to cross the Huzhuang River Bridge, there is a black-painted gatehouse, and they never fail to mention the tall black dog in front of the gate, as tall as a stone lion. The black dog is the sign of the Zhu Country Gentleman's house. It spends all day squatting under the screen wall outside the black-painted gate, its pair of blue eyes vigilantly scrutinizing every traveler coming and going on the Huzhuang Bridge. When a regular visitor comes to visit the Country Gentleman, the black dog has already nimbly scurried into the gatehouse to tell the old gatekeeper, who has served the Zhu family for three generations. The old gatekeeper suffers from a chronic cough and relies on the history of his family serving for three generations to eat this ready-made meal in the Zhu mansion. The black dog was originally raised by the young master for hunting, but for the sake of the tenants, it also took on the job of the old gatekeeper's assistant, so the old gatekeeper loved it even more than the young master.

The black dog is said to be a wolf breed, with a wolf-like head, erect ears, and strong legs. After the Huzhuang Bridge is raised at night, it can scurry back and forth across the two-zhang-wide river. The purchase price was three hundred taels of silver, which was a much-talked-about story in this town at the time. The dog's appetite is even more astonishing, requiring five sheng of white rice and five catties of beef a day, which a young servant named A Gen is dedicated to providing. The black dog, having such a great history, has also solved a shocking and strange case, which is that it scurried up the roof and captured a robber. Therefore, when mentioning the Zhu Country Gentleman, no one dares to leave out the black dog.

This autumn, once, when the young master returned from hunting, the black dog suddenly disappeared. The young servant A Gen almost didn't eat or sleep for two days, searching in nearby towns. Later, an old man delivered it to the gate of the Zhu mansion, saying that the black dog was sleeping in his cattle pen. After the young master rewarded the old man, he ordered A Gen to chain the black dog with an iron chain. He no longer took the dog with him when hunting. But when the black dog saw the young master go out, it always barked and howled, jumping up as high as a person, and the iron chain seemed about to break. The Zhu Country Gentleman is quite superstitious. He thought that something unlucky was about to happen, so he still took it out when hunting, or even stopped hunting altogether, and let it guard the gate under the screen wall steadily. But the young master didn't listen to his father's words!

"Dad, don't worry. That dog is too sensitive. It can smell my scent from miles away. It follows me everywhere every day. Now that it's locked up, it naturally barks and jumps when it knows I'm going out. But if it disappears again like last time, not to mention the hundreds of taels of silver, you can't buy such a good dog for a while."

The father loves his son, so naturally he no longer pays attention to the dog. Moreover, the father has his own affairs to attend to. The young master still went out hunting every day, but he specially instructed the young servant A Gen to be wary of the black dog. The dog was chained beside the stone lion during the day and locked in A Gen's room at night. The old gatekeeper naturally grumbled, because he loved the dog, and after the dog was locked up, when he heard it shouting outside the long gate, he had to come out of the gatehouse with his cane, fearing that a distinguished guest would come to visit the Country Gentleman.

Despite such strict precautions, one morning it bit through the iron chain and disappeared again, but the young master who went out hunting was beaten and carried back in the afternoon, and the dog followed behind with its head drooping.

Since it was an affair in the Zhu Country Gentleman's house, the next day this news spread throughout the town.

It turned out that the young master had forcibly taken a married woman in a neighboring town. That day, the black dog howled loudly beside the woman's bamboo fence, attracting the attention of the neighbors, thus discovering the young master's affair and being beaten badly by them.

Although the Zhu Country Gentleman immediately called the local security chief to pay a sum of money, the news had spread everywhere like the wind. The Zhu Country Gentleman therefore vented his anger on the black dog, tied a stone to it, and sank it in the Huzhuang River, and the young servant A Gen also broke his rice bowl as a result.

Sparrow

— Man Yin

There is an unknown evergreen tree in the yard, it is an old tree of many years. This year, when renovating the courtyard, the family members ordered the craftsmen to kill it because it could not blossom and bear fruit, and its appearance was not very elegant (like a hunchbacked old man crouching in the corner of the wall, and a huge branch like Feilai Peak stood high outside the wall). I love flowers and trees very much. Although I have never grafted a flower or turned over a pot, I hope that flowers will bloom in the yard all year round. However, once winter comes, the yard is like a lonely cemetery. All kinds of flowers and plants that were once thriving have been moved into the flower room, and only that not very elegant evergreen tree stubbornly survives in the cold wind. In winter, being able to see a bit of verdant green can dispel the melancholy like gloomy days. That's why I opposed replacing that evergreen tree, so I changed it by cutting off that deformed giant branch and letting it crouch in the corner of the wall. It was then that I discovered a sparrow's nest securely built among the dense leaves. It is said that pigeons and magpies occupy nests, and sparrows are even more cowardly, hiding under people's eaves or among the tiles of ancient temples and deserted pagodas. The sparrow's nest on that evergreen tree, although far less neat and delicate than a swallow's nest, simply collects some fallen leaves and broken branches and builds a prototype at the intersection of the branches. But I think it's a miracle. Since I discovered this secret, I have stood in front of the window every day, like a philosophical researcher, examining the group of sparrows jumping in the yard and on the roof. After spending many days, I did not find anything special about that group of sparrows. They played all day and stole a little food around my house's chicken coop. I also visited their nest several times, but it was never completely repaired. Those fallen leaves and broken branches gradually rotted, and that prototype nest barely just waited for the branches to support it. After my research failed, I stopped paying attention to it. Recently, there was a mix of wind and snow, which broke off a branch, and the sparrow's nest was about to overturn. That group of sparrows all avoided coming to the front of the window. They were trembling and chirping, like a group of refugees. After a day and night, some of them even died of stiffness. Those who did not die were still trembling and chirping. My younger brother caught them one by one in birdcages, fed them rice and millet, and gave them clear water to drink. After hanging them in the house for less than half a day, they recovered their normal state and jumped and played in the cages. They forgot the horror of winter, forgot the pain of the overturned nest, or perhaps they were even singing the birdcage, the current place of comfort

There is a fable about bees and sparrows in elementary school textbooks: One winter, a sparrow borrowed grain from a bee, and the bee replied: "You play in the spring, play in the summer, play in the autumn. My grain is prepared for myself to spend the winter." Sparrows are lazy and procrastinating. I previously thought that it was my mistake that they could build nests. They cannot invade magpies' nests like doves, nor can they prepare for winter in advance and store grain. After the nest is overturned, they are still frozen to death if they live under other people's eaves. Well, these current birdcages, they naturally regard them as comfortable nests. (Winter Essays II)

Broadcasting

Song Introduction

Remember My Love in the Xiang River Waves

At that time, I was drunk with a beautiful woman, the beauty's color was as delicate as a flower, today the beauty abandons me, in the brothel pearl curtain at the end of the sky, the beauty is like Chang'e in the moon, three or five, two eight, full and lacking. Green eyebrows like cicada wings, a life of separation, a heart broken from not seeing each other. Heart broken, I wake up with tears dripping into the Xiang River, the Xiang River is deep on both sides, the beauty is not seen, a sad heart, playing the lute with sorrow, the tune is high and the string breaks, no confidant, beauty oh beauty, I don't know if you are evening rain or morning clouds, thinking of you all night, plum blossoms bloom suddenly, I suddenly suspect it is you.

At that time, I was moored overseas, the beauty's appearance was as bright as a flower, at this moment, I return home to see the beauty, but the person is gone and the building is empty, tears like rain, the graceful beauty is gone, how can I not miss her? The pale white sleeves are so delicate, once gone, never to return, there's nothing I can do, there's nothing I can do, remembering you, I'm still drunk, singing the white-haired poem with sorrow, telling my confidant in the tune of the lute, beauty oh beauty, I don't know if you are evening rain or morning clouds, thinking of you all night, deep dreams are long, remember my love in the Xiang River waves.

National Studies

Feng Ming Le Guwen Guanzhi

Li Shude (940) 7:30 AM to 8:30 AM

Topic: Quyuanchun's Hall Notes (II)

I heard this, and suddenly had a premonition. It is true that everything in life is caused by fate. I only remember the name "West Lake Chief," which originated from Su Shi. Su Shi had West Lake both when he guarded Hangzhou and Yingzhou. Therefore, when he arrived in Yingzhou to thank the Executive Yuan, he wrote, "Entering the two prohibitions, I have often tarnished the glory of the North Gate. As a local official in two states, I have repeatedly been the Chief of West Lake." Later, he was demoted to Huizhou, and there was also West Lake there. Therefore, Chen Chengzi's poem said, "Su Shi originally had a West Lake Chief, but he could not rest without going to Luofu." In that case, only those like Yu Weinong, who have served in this land, are entitled to call themselves that. This seal does not seem to be something that hermits should use. However, in this dynasty, there was a poet-monk Zheng Yan who wrote a poem in the style of Dianjiangchun, saying, "Coming and going through the smoke and waves, this life is called the West Lake Chief." If a Buddhist monk can call himself that, then we may also have no objection. Therefore, I wrote a poem in the style of Moshanxi, the first line of which is, "Wandering with books and swords, I am old and a West Lake Chief." Living in it without doubt, it's quite amusing.

It is truly a wonderful piece of entertainment during Christmas, full of pleasing songs, moving dances, and lighthearted humor, which can intoxicate the audience for two hours. The leading actor is Dick Powell, who is a veteran of musical films. His past works, such as "Moon Over Miami", still leave a good impression in the minds of movie fans. In addition, jazz king Paul Whiteman leads his entire orchestra to join the collaboration, which is like icing on the cake, making this film even more musical. The left picture shows Paul Whiteman's orchestra.

The plot, performance, and background of the film are all excellent. At the same time, they are also showing the timely color cartoon "The Night Before Christmas."

Shanghai Shenbao Local Supplement Automobile Weekly

New Trends in Automobile Design at the Earls Court Motor Show

— Zhenmin

At this year's Earls Court Motor Show, there were 59 participating car manufacturers, including 30 from the UK, 15 from the US, and the remaining 14 from continental Europe. The novelty of the car styles, the high efficiency of the engines, and the safety of driving were truly deeply satisfying and unprecedented in previous exhibitions, and worthy of our attention.

The streamlined design of car bodies has now entered a regulated state. The previously unrestrained car styles are difficult to find at the exhibition, because engineers have made further progress in the study of air resistance. The value of the drag coefficient has been newly determined, so the streamline design of any part of the car body is now much more precise. Furthermore, special consideration is now given to the volume of the passenger compartment, seeking appropriate proportions, which is completely different from the one-sided streamlining of the past.

All-steel car roofs were once the most fashionable, but they are now gradually being replaced by aluminum alloy ones. This new type of roof is not only aesthetically pleasing, but also extremely light, which can reduce the weight of the car body. It is also more economical and can save the cost of external paint.

Independent springs were heavily criticized by many engineers in the recent past, but they have recently been completely successful. At this exhibition, 66 percent of the cars displayed by the US and continental Europe did not have front axles. British cars probably have an even larger percentage. In these cars, the front wheels are supported by radius arms and transverse springs. The two wheels are not connected, so that the distribution of the car body's weight is more even. The vibration during driving is almost completely avoided, and repairs are also much easier.

The weight of the car body's skeleton is gradually being reduced, because strong and flexible special steel skeletons are gradually being adopted. The entire car bottom has now been successfully cast, which is truly a new record in the history of automobiles. However, because the cost is too high, it has not yet been widely adopted. Currently, most of the car body's joints must be welded, and its strength is several times greater than the old method of riveting. Therefore, it is almost impossible to find joints on the current new car skeleton.

The design of engines is now largely based on the operation of aircraft engines, and more comprehensive consideration is given. The amount of oil used per mile has been reduced to a minimum, and the piston stroke has gradually been increased to expand horsepower. Because the number of engine revolutions per minute is increasing, the work of the radiator is becoming increasingly important. The latest air and water radiators have been successfully adopted. In the past, engines could not transmit increased power after shifting gears (that is, changing speeds), resulting in a large loss, which was the most uneconomical thing. Now, the design of the gearbox has been changed to reduce losses significantly.

The most satisfying thing about new cars is the use of hydraulic power to automatically adjust the gaps in the valve mechanism, which is enough to make driving safer and more economical. This new device was not easy to design, and it was truly the result of joint research by all engineers. The radiator and crankshaft box have adopted integral sand casting, making the movement more sensitive. The lubrication system of each part of the engine is almost completely automated, and the lubrication areas of each part are more precise and effective, which is enough to promote the good operation of the engine.

The change of power transmission will be easier. Now a newer gear system has been invented. The "Thunderbolt" on the "Hudson" car has achieved amazing results. In this system, the speed change is completely done by the effect of current and vacuum. When applied, you only need to press the electric button to get the required action, which is extremely convenient.

The design of the passenger compartment is now gradually being entrusted to specialized engineers (separated from the car body design). Comfort and artistic beauty will be achieved. A new car with glass windows all around will be displayed. The advantage of this car is that it allows people in the passenger compartment to easily see and appreciate the scenery, especially when driving in the countryside.

The engine position will be further forward in the car body, while the rear of the car body will be more extended, and the bottom of the car will be closer to the ground, making the position of the passenger compartment more spacious. All of this is enough to increase the comfort and satisfaction of driving.

Judging by the results at this year's motor show, British cars probably occupy the most advantageous position. Among them, cars such as "Hillman" and "Humber" are impressively designed, with excellent construction, giving people a deep impression. Others such as "Alvis" and "Talbot" are also exquisite and agile, truly excellent structures. Of course, the "Ford" is the fastest growing of the new American cars, but in recent years, car manufacturers have been competing hard, and there has been more rapid progress in design and construction. There must be amazing results at this exhibition.

Statistics of US Automobile Accidents

36,000 Injured in 1934, Nearly 40,000 Expected in 1935

Not long ago, there was an article in this publication translating the statistics of automobile accidents in the United Kingdom. However, in some places, the UK's records were compared. According to the statistics of government agencies, in 1934, 36,000 people were killed by cars throughout the United States. As for this year, although accurate statistics are not yet available, many people believe that it will increase to 40,000, because the record of automobile accidents has been increasing rapidly in recent months. Nervous people believe that this situation is enough to reflect the recovery of the automobile industry, because at the height of the economic crisis, there were at least three to four million cars in the United States that were parked in garages because the owners did not have money to buy gasoline. Not only are these cars now being driven, but they are also increasing the number of miles driven. Two other reasons for the increase in accident records are the increase in speed and the fact that many drunk people have been driving since the end of Prohibition. According to statistical experts, the record of automobile accidents in the United States is not very high in fact. According to statistics in 1932, 21.9 people per 1,000,000 people in the United States were killed by cars, while that year it was 9.9 people in the UK. However, we must know that in the United States, there is an average of one car for every 5.25 people, while in the UK, there is only one car for every 25 people.

The record of deaths caused by automobile accidents is increasing, although it is due to the increasing number of car users, but in terms of proportion, it is probably far exceeding it. Between 1933 and 1934, the amount of gasoline consumed by cars in the United States increased by 7 percent, but fatal accident cases increased by 13 percent. In history, this record is the highest. The increase in records is much worse in the suburbs than in the cities. Perhaps city residents, whether pedestrians or drivers, have received a lot of lessons about avoiding accidents. They are cautious in walking and driving. The most common disaster is the collision of two cars, accounting for 43.3 percent of the total number of accidents. The second most common is the collision between cars and pedestrians, accounting for 38.3 percent. This may be unexpected. Accidents that do not involve collisions account for only 5.3 percent. The loss of life is much less in car-to-car collisions than in car-to-person collisions. The former accounts for only 23.8 percent, while the latter accounts for 44.3 percent. In 1934, a total of 954,000 people in the United States were injured by cars but not fatally. Although these accident cases include those caused by drunk driving, the record is increasing daily. But we cannot say that drunkenness is an important reason for the increase in automobile accidents, because in automobile accident cases, only 5 to 10 percent of drivers or pedestrians are mistaken due to alcohol. On this ratio, we really cannot point out that drunkenness is an important factor in increasing the accident record.

In recent years, some cities in the United States have started from the educational aspect to reduce the record of vehicle accidents. As a result, considerable success has been achieved, because in the midst of the national increase in records, those cities are decreasing. Take San Francisco, California, as an example. During the period when the number of fatal cases increased by 13 percent nationwide, it decreased by 15 percent. Pittsburgh, Pennsylvania, decreased by 13 percent during the same period. Recently, in order to reduce the accident record, the United States has adopted the method of inspecting all cars on the market at least once a year. Brakes, headlights, and other mechanisms must be inspected. If any defects are found, the car owner must be asked to repair them immediately to ensure driving safety. In some cities, the police in one area compete with the police in another area. As a result of maintaining traffic order, the accident record in that area is lower. Statistics are compiled once a week or month. Those who achieve good results are rewarded by the authorities. In this way, the police treat the drivers who cause accidents as enemies, and within the scope of possibility, they try to prevent automobile accidents. In some places, young people formally have a course in automobile driving in high schools for practice. Because in the United States, all children know how to drive a car by the time they are twelve or thirteen years old, so in fact they already know how to drive a car at that time. However, bad habits are corrected in school, and various operating principles of internal combustion engines are taught.

There is still a big shortcoming in the United States, which is that there is no unified traffic rule nationwide. All traffic regulations are formulated by each state. The rules on the road, even the police's gestures and the traffic lights at intersections, are different from state to state. Therefore, many disasters are caused by drivers not understanding these rules. In half of the states, driving a car does not require a license, and there is no minimum age limit. The accident record in these places is one-third higher than in strict places. In states where a driver's license is required, people sit in the car with the police officer when they go to take the test. They must first drive a lot of roads in the busy area, and then test the skills of turning and parking on a slope at the foot of a mountain. At the same time, they must be asked about various traffic rules and check whether their eyesight is good. People who apply for a license may pass the second or third time, but most of them fail the first time. In terms of the number of drivers nationwide, the United States is indeed the country with the lowest accident record. If a person causes a certain number of accidents while driving, the license will be revoked as usual. But someone suggested that such people should hang a huge white license plate on the car so that other drivers know that his driving skills are immature and that he needs a lot of space to drive the vehicle.

In the United States, in addition to the authorities, car manufacturers have recently joined forces to reduce the record of automobile accidents. Many new cars have been equipped with unbreakable glass. Even tires that are insured not to burst in the middle of the road have been discovered on the market. All new cars now have a lower gravity than old cars. Therefore, there are many fewer cases of collisions with trains, because most of these intersections do not have safety equipment, except for a part of these intersections with watchmen or wire gates. Therefore, car accidents easily occur when trains pass. Therefore, US President Roosevelt once advocated removing some of these intersections, and the road administration should also bear part of the expenses to prevent accidents. Comparing the driving course with the accident record, night is much more than day. The only reason is that the driver's eyesight is not good at night, and the headlights of oncoming cars are too strong, making it difficult for people to open their eyes. Therefore, some places have banned the use of strong headlights at night, or asked drivers to dim the lights when they see an oncoming car. Recently, someone invented a highway headlight that allows people to see the light even during the day. Because it uses gas light, it is very safe even if the vehicle is driven very fast. It is also safe not to use headlights in the dark.

In a country where there are 25 million of their buses, buses, and trucks, it is indeed not an easy task for the authorities to maintain traffic safety. Therefore, in university teaching, traffic management has now been included in the formal curriculum to train this talent. Recently, the United States invented a "double wave system" to manage traffic. This system has been tried on Michigan Avenue in Chicago. Under this new system, the speed of driving is not allowed to exceed 30 miles per hour. Seeing the red light at the intersection turning into a green light, even if the traffic is congested, you can boldly move forward without stopping. This system is implemented on a road in two Rui. In addition, there is another method, which is a police car equipped with a sound transmitter. Each car has two police officers, one driving and one observing. They patrol on the road. The person observing has a very high sound transmitter in front of him. The cars half a mile away can also hear what he says. The police car patrols on the street. Seeing that some drivers do not follow the rules and fail to self-examine, they will be warned to make people pay attention. Therefore, seeing this police car passing by, the driver will pay special attention, and hearing the sound of warning others from afar will also alert himself. This is not necessarily a new method to prevent accidents.

Grand Opening of the Lincoln Zephyr Car Exhibition

On November 2, 193_?, the latest products of the automobile industry, the Lincoln Zephyr and Lincoln cars, were publicly displayed for the first day at the Astor Hotel in New York City. More than 61,000 people were attracted to visit.

This Zephyr car is the latest product in the mid-price car category. It is the result of the joint efforts and resources of the Ford Motor Company and the Lincoln Motor Company. Whether it is the appearance or engineering design, everything is novel and adopts the most advanced concepts. All the principles used have never been put into practice in the automobile production industry.

This car is equipped with a newly developed 110-horsepower V-12 engine. Its appearance is the most perfectly streamlined among mass-produced cars. It is also the first car made in the American continent without using a car frame or chassis. The car body is an all-steel "bridge-linked" type, with extraordinary strength. The installation of the engine is right in it. The moving gears are also attached to it.

The display at the Astor Hotel also included Ford A8 trucks and commercial vehicles. A total of 42 vehicles were displayed. At the same time, the same vehicles were displayed at the Ford retail showroom in New York. On the first day, a total of 22,000 people actually arrived. And the smaller-scale passenger car display held at the Park Lane Hotel had 7,000 people. The Astor Hotel also shows a moving picture introducing the new Zephyr car every day. There are 3,000 viewers every day.

The Problem of Lubrication for Automobile Machinery

— Little Ang

Generally, the friction between two machine parts, even to a slight degree, results in nothing more than the heating of the parts and the wearing down of the materials. Taking automobiles as an example, the material worn away by the brakes alone can reach tens of thousands of tons annually. The consumption of other capabilities is certainly significant. The use of lubricating oil is precisely to reduce this problem. When any smooth metal surface is viewed under a microscope, it appears uneven with bumps and dents. The lubricating oil used between two machine parts is stored in these areas, fulfilling its lubricating function. Sometimes, the oil can also be absorbed by the metal, giving it a glassy sheen. This phenomenon is commonly seen inside cylinders.

There are many types of lubricating oil, and their applications also vary. Briefly, they are discussed below.

Lubrication of crankshafts and bearings: When the crankshaft is rotating, due to the wedge effect, the shaft body rises, resulting in the highest and lowest pressure points between them. The lubricating oil should be added at the point of lowest pressure. The principle is very clear. (A) Types of Lubricators: Those used for crankshafts and bearings include: (a) Oil hole: A hole is drilled in the bearing, and oil is added to it from time to time. (b) Siphon: A cotton yarn strip with one end immersed in lubricating oil and the other end placed above the shaft, allowing drops to fall intermittently onto the shaft. (c) Needle Lubricator: A small gap is often left between the shaft and the bearing, which causes vibration during operation, thereby activating a needle-shaped valve in the lubricator. This allows lubricating oil to flow out. When the crankshaft is stationary, the needle drops due to gravity, preventing oil leakage. Because of this adjustment, it is more economical than the previous two. (d) Chain: A chain is placed around the shaft, with the lower end immersed in lubricating oil. As the chain rotates, it carries the lubricating oil upwards. (e) Collar: Its function is the same as above, but it replaces the chain with a collar. (f) Mechanical Lubricator: The lubricating oil is forced by a pump, forming a circulating system. The used oil is filtered and can be reused. Moreover, the heat generated by the bearing can also be dissipated through the circulation of the lubricating oil. This is the most economical and effective lubricator. It is widely used in machines of all sizes.

Cylinders and Pistons: The engine's power is sometimes reduced by as much as 10% due to the resistance between the cylinders and pistons. Insufficient lubrication can be heard as a rough, grating noise from within the cylinders. The lubricator used for this is the Hydrostatic Lubricator, which uses the pressure of condensed water to achieve lubrication. Another type uses injectors. In essence, the goal is to form tiny oil droplets that mix with the steam and adhere to the cylinder and piston. Mixed oil is commonly used, but it should not be used in steam engines with condensers. Only mineral oil should be used.

The types of lubricating oil and their application methods have been described above. Special attention should be paid to the selection of lubricating oil for automobile machinery. In short, the better the lubricating oil, the longer the life of the car, and the faster the speed. Long-distance travel becomes more comfortable. Automobile owners should pay attention to this.
